id='poem_content_1376310'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376310'>段章者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376310_comment'></div>不知何许人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376310_comment'></div>咸通十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376310_comment'></div>吾中第在京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376310_comment'></div>章以自僦为驭者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376310_comment'></div>亦无异于他佣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376310_comment'></div>夏归蒲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376310_comment'></div>久之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376310_comment'></div>力不足以赒给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376310_comment'></div>乃谢去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376310_comment'></div>广明庚子岁冬十二月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376310_comment'></div>寇犯京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376310_comment'></div>愚居崇义里九日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376310_comment'></div>自<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1376310", 1376310, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>里豪</span>杨琼所转匿常平廪下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376310_comment'></div>将出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376310_comment'></div>群盗继至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376310_comment'></div>有拥戈拒门者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376310_comment'></div>熟视良久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376310_comment'></div>乃就持吾手曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376310_comment'></div>某段章也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376310_comment'></div>系虏而来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376310_comment'></div>未能自脱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376310_comment'></div>然<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1376310", 1376310, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>顾怀</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1376310", 1376310, "Clauses/22/Comments/1")'>优养</span>之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376310_comment'></div>今乃相遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376310_comment'></div>天也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376310_comment'></div>某所主张将军喜下士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376310_comment'></div>且幸偕往通他。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376310_comment'></div>不且仆藉于渫𨌑中矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376310_comment'></div>愚誓不以辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376310_comment'></div>章惘然泣下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376310_comment'></div>导至通衢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376310_comment'></div>即别去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376310_comment'></div>愚因此得自开远门宵遁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376310_comment'></div>至咸阳桥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376310_comment'></div>复榜者韩钧济之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376310_comment'></div>乃抵鄠县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376310_comment'></div>赞曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376310_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_1376310'>时方治平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376310_comment'></div>士君子足以相济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376310_comment'></div>而祸乱之作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376310_comment'></div>必厮役者乃能脱事患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376310_comment'></div>古人所以安不易危耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376310_comment'></div>且章之服役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376310_comment'></div>吾待以常佣耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376310_comment'></div>及滨于死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376310_comment'></div>竟赖其义而获免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376310_comment'></div>安知他日吾属报及其所奉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376310_comment'></div>果致不愧于尔曹耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376310_comment'></div>乃志于篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_11938_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_11939' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_11939' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/11939?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_11939'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_11939'>景阳楼下花钿镜，玄武湖边锦绣旗。<div id='poem_sentence_0_11939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_11939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_11939'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_11939_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_11940' class='authorDate'>（881年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_11940_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_11940'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_11940'>乱后人间尽不平，秦川花木最伤情。<div id='poem_sentence_0_11940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_11940'>无穷红艳红尘里，骤马分香散入营。<div id='poem_sentence_1_11940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_11940'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_11940_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=882&endYear=882')">882年11月</a>　王徽受召镇潞，乃表图为副使，因徽不赴镇而止。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=883&endYear=883')">883年</a>　约本年六七月，图奉敕为河中节度使王重荣撰《解县新城碑》<div id='poem_1376301' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376301' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376301?labeling=true' target='_blank'>解县新城碑<span class='inlineComment2'>（奉敕撰）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（883年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14662, "唐末", "司空图", "poem_title_1376301")'>司空图</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376301_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376301'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376301'>夫披图著象。即亘长垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376301_comment'></div>裂壤奠居。必扃峻阀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376301_comment'></div>虽四邻之可恃。在百雉之难窥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376301_comment'></div>然而事有弛张。得时而后显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376301_comment'></div>功无巨细。得人而后施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376301_comment'></div>今见之于解城矣。我皇帝之御宇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376301_comment'></div>累圣勤求。登贤致乂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376301_comment'></div>凿乾缔搆。允归睿作之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376301_comment'></div>寿国<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1376301", 1376301, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>陶融</span>。必有挺生之佐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376301_comment'></div>式扶昌运。对越上元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376301_comment'></div>皇帝体睿哲之机。延统和之祚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376301_comment'></div>高视无外。旁罗不遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376301_comment'></div>洪水安澜。格兹穹壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376301_comment'></div>明廷委瑞。分映古今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376301_comment'></div>肃清庙之威灵。竭大臣之忠力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376301_comment'></div>虽钟灾会。益振英图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376301_comment'></div>系在知人。念兹活国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376301_comment'></div>内则皋夔叶赞。外则方召专征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376301_comment'></div>克著庙谟。且贞师律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376301_comment'></div>其有兼膺注意。宜属宏材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376301_comment'></div>正柱石于洪基。感风云于冥数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376301_comment'></div>盖祥发神授。佑我昌期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376301_comment'></div>斯人见之于蒲帅司徒王公矣。西爽炳灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376301_comment'></div>中条会秀。致用则牢笼三杰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376301_comment'></div>图功则拟议一匡。受寄股肱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376301_comment'></div>佥谐梦卜。遇帝车出狩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376301_comment'></div>天邑缠兵。邓禹则封拜关中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376301_comment'></div>方之未重。寇恂则抚绥河内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376301_comment'></div>比此宁艰。辍外师之稔谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376301_comment'></div>导邻藩之叶举。于是使星远降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376301_comment'></div>诏命始通。瞻日月而惟新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376301_comment'></div>觉山河之自固。人祇洞感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376301_comment'></div>军旅益雄。但既逼寇仇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376301_comment'></div>且当津要。车徒遝至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376301_comment'></div>竟赴齐盟。戎夏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_34_1376301", 1376301, "Clauses/69/Comments/0")'>骏驱</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376301_comment'></div>共匡京室。虑风回于原燎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376301_comment'></div>竭日费于云屯。辑睦允谐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376301_comment'></div>克赡栋□持广厦。鼎镇厚坤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376301_comment'></div>始以一城之危。抗<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_1376301", 1376301, "Clauses/77/Comments/0")'>移国</span>之盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376301_comment'></div>竟以数郡之力。壮勤王之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376301_comment'></div>勋复旧都。庆延殊渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376301_comment'></div>盛矣哉。传曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376301_comment'></div>德刑具举。武之经也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376301_comment'></div>农战交修。政之本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376301_comment'></div>总是数者。方为全美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376301_comment'></div>此府自大历贞元之隆。郭公浑公继临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376301_comment'></div>虽博厚<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_1376301", 1376301, "Clauses/92/Comments/0")'>粹和</span>。本朝实赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376301_comment'></div>而俭德异政。旧史阙然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376301_comment'></div>公<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_48_1376301", 1376301, "Clauses/96/Comments/0")'>洞识</span>古今。兼资文武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376301_comment'></div>宏以济物。而恕必探情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376301_comment'></div>明以照奸。而杀惟制乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1376301_comment'></div>人皆知耻。道不拾遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1376301_comment'></div>视礼法之率由。信恩威之并济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1376301_comment'></div>犹以为备则无患。志在格言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1376301_comment'></div>安则怀生。命于善教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1376301_comment'></div>是资蔽恶。有待必攻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1376301_comment'></div>晋人之固护河南。齐将之经营汾北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1376301_comment'></div>虽谋非善守。难婴战角之晨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1376301_comment'></div>而利有必争。宜保马头之险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1376301_comment'></div>由是公之初莅镇也。即以此地北绵汾晋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1376301_comment'></div>西逼界秦。造陇而虽贯复关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1376301_comment'></div>压境而匪凭高垒。时当无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1376301_comment'></div>则鸡犬混并。运属有戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1376301_comment'></div>则豺狼密迩。浮罂或渡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1376301_comment'></div>萦带是虞。遂刱新规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1376301_comment'></div>骤成坚垒。挟洪荒而作固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1376301_comment'></div>屹断岸以高临。事等振喉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1376301_comment'></div>势同捍首。岂比平原伐陇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1376301_comment'></div>自标威寇之名。斛律侵周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1376301_comment'></div>别建定夷之号。及城陷冯翊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1376301_comment'></div>西面益孤。烽举隰州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1376301_comment'></div>北军方至。迁延未测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1376301_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_72_1376301", 1376301, "Clauses/144/Comments/0")'>侦谍</span>相摇。日有风传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1376301_comment'></div>士无人色。赖我关防夹峙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1376301_comment'></div>津戍旁通。杜两岸之金汤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1376301_comment'></div>坚众心之铁石。共增声势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1376301_comment'></div>得以枝梧。既纳款于帅臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1376301_comment'></div>仍抚安其新附。交获利济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1376301_comment'></div>并致成功。不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1376301_comment'></div>所恃长川。亦当夺险矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1376301_comment'></div>而又以解因沃饶之润。置搉货之司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1376301_comment'></div>官帑委输。商徒繁会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1376301_comment'></div>云连里闬。山峙赀财。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1376301_comment'></div>弦歌讵称于武城。锦绣惭誇于襄邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1376301_comment'></div>贯天钱而下积。已应星文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1376301_comment'></div>认宝气而旁瞻。非惟剑气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1376301_comment'></div>所患者。素无城守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1376301_comment'></div>难固人心。微有警于烟氛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1376301_comment'></div>遽深藏于林鹳。孰惩诲盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1376301_comment'></div>克让周防。振古所遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1376301_comment'></div>非公莫集。既总两河之务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1376301_comment'></div>值多事之秋。检吏通商。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1376301_comment'></div>机能制用。矫时阜俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1376301_comment'></div>俭以率先。凡立科条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1376301_comment'></div>皆能刻励。五使虽优于兼俸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1376301_comment'></div>一毫不润于私家。用给工徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1376301_comment'></div>遂兴板筑。精择主将得张郁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1376301_comment'></div>时官聚军雠。市摇物估。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1376301_comment'></div>欲因赋役。亦以赈饥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1376301_comment'></div>夫事贵研深。所以见于未兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1376301_comment'></div>人难虑始。所以乐于视成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1376301_comment'></div>初公密计地宜。且稽农隙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1376301_comment'></div>裁其经纬。授以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_102_1376301", 1376301, "Clauses/205/Comments/0")'>规绳</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1376301_comment'></div>吏既克勤。期不愆素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1376301_comment'></div>自中和二年冬十月。奏请兴役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1376301_comment'></div>至明年夏六月。凡计工五十万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1376301_comment'></div>城高三丈。周绕九里一百六十步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1376301_comment'></div>隍刳浚洫。堞冠层楼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1376301_comment'></div>外刱犒军之营。内修御敌之具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1376301_comment'></div>观其地萦壮址。云郁平川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1376301_comment'></div>拥形势而增严。屏要冲而莫犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1376301_comment'></div>归师远迹。忘自意于窥觎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1376301_comment'></div>匝境罢扃。亦宁虞于奔窜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1376301_comment'></div>其他缉饰。悉叶机宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1376301_comment'></div>公旋陟上台。恳辞剧务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1376301_comment'></div>咸欣庇赖。益著咏歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1376301_comment'></div>遂乞飞章。愿刊殊绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1376301_comment'></div>以图同庥乐土。见托芜词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1376301_comment'></div>榷盐使韦雍。检律在公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1376301_comment'></div>巡官王悫。琢磨效用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1376301_comment'></div>与植将及商人等。联状同诣所居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1376301_comment'></div>沥恳至于垂涕。窃惟自古恢扬盛业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1376301_comment'></div>激赞宏图。朝则带砺传盟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1376301_comment'></div>家则<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_123_1376301", 1376301, "Clauses/246/Comments/0")'>盘盂</span>著誓。必资麟笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1376301_comment'></div>共振鲸钟。虽代积峥嵘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1376301_comment'></div>而声棱悠久。沧溟<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_125_1376301", 1376301, "Clauses/251/Comments/0")'>鳌抃</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1376301_comment'></div>日观可危。片石螭衔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1376301_comment'></div>云台永峙。将贻终古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1376301_comment'></div>实在斯文。雅非振藻之工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1376301_comment'></div>敢徇披丹之款。榷盐使崔赞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1376301_comment'></div>温恭奉上。感励知催。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1376301_comment'></div>勘使王能遵。妙简宸衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1376301_comment'></div>喜成王事。并以磨砻已久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1376301_comment'></div>结搆仍崇。靡知跼地之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1376301_comment'></div>遽有闻天之请。名微墨客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1376301_comment'></div>短才本谢于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_135_1376301", 1376301, "Clauses/270/Comments/0")'>徼能</span>。事僭词臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1376301_comment'></div>牢让岂申于恭命。且禁暴曰治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1376301_comment'></div>济众曰仁。以此视其为诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1376301_comment'></div>足以知其为政。众惟同仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1376301_comment'></div>暴莫可凌。彼或蔽捍边荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1376301_comment'></div>缮修保障。犹誇溢美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1376301_comment'></div>显示将来。况数仞耸威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1376301_comment'></div>近函陜右。一方增气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1376301_comment'></div>旁带关河。储国用于无虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1376301_comment'></div>息人劳于永逸。宠传褒诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1376301_comment'></div>喜动邻封。方属沈绵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1376301_comment'></div>难辞<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_146_1376301", 1376301, "Clauses/292/Comments/0")'>纪述</span>。与崇墉而并揭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1376301_comment'></div>岂深谷之我迁。式备昭功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1376301_comment'></div>靡惭摭实。铭云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1376301_comment'></div>蒲乃国枢。佥惟天作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1376301_comment'></div>挟魏控秦。佩河冠岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1376301_comment'></div>蒲屏是雄。勋贤是托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1376301_comment'></div>孰膺帝俞。克振王略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1376301_comment'></div>上哲倚注。元臣激扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1376301_comment'></div>干霄作镇。跨海为梁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1376301_comment'></div>令无不肃。谋无不臧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1376301_comment'></div>擢彼新垒。屹然巨防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1376301_comment'></div>川广可踰。山高可轹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1376301_comment'></div>曷以善闭。必资全策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1376301_comment'></div>城隍增严。晨惊夕惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1376301_comment'></div>利害斯睹。天悬壤隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1376301_comment'></div>解宝近盐。货则兼赢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1376301_comment'></div>车喧咽轧。户侈连甍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1376301_comment'></div>财雄擅响。鼎食提衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1376301_comment'></div>三河竞凑。六辅皆倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1376301_comment'></div>内贯通庄。外无固圉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1376301_comment'></div>易戒致戎。书警纳侮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1376301_comment'></div>或骇一呼。难施九拒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1376301_comment'></div>虽有栋榱。谁庇风雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1376301_comment'></div>传褒命日。诗美维翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1376301_comment'></div>长空岳耸。厚地云蟠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1376301_comment'></div>俸能兼济。众得怀安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1376301_comment'></div>圣衷乃眷。茂迹宜刊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1376301_comment'></div>兆叶人谋。机先神授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1376301_comment'></div>虞于不虞。守其必守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1376301_comment'></div>峻亦不夷。坚亦不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1376301_comment'></div>唯此殊功。翊之克久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1376301_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_177_1376301_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=883&endYear=883')">883年</a>　图又应王重荣、王重盈之情为其父王纵作《追述碑》<div id='poem_1376305' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376305' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376305?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故盐州防御使王纵追述碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（883年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14662, "唐末", "司空图", "poem_title_1376305")'>司空图</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376305_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376305'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376305'>夫爽贯五行。粲星芒而腾列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376305_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1376305", 1376305, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>灵标</span>万汇。挺人杰以降祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376305_comment'></div>式赞鸿钧。乃符元感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376305_comment'></div>恒运絪缊之化。潜融橐籥之和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376305_comment'></div>然而拂日贞松。必生于乔岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376305_comment'></div>环天重器。亦铸于洪炉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376305_comment'></div>水积厚而脱鹏。门愈高而容驷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376305_comment'></div>克蕃令绪。固在华宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376305_comment'></div>况自缑岭上征。姬邦委驭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376305_comment'></div>代为著姓。人不乏贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376305_comment'></div>或<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1376305", 1376305, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>济美</span>于参墟。或炳灵于沂水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376305_comment'></div>祥分铁印。系总璇源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376305_comment'></div>西晋殊勋。则荣连邸第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376305_comment'></div>北朝雅望。则地显官婚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376305_comment'></div>贻谋各著于承家。致用皆光其佐命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376305_comment'></div>朱轮华冕。岂独推恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376305_comment'></div>甲令门风。实先种德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376305_comment'></div>是资奕叶。谁与提衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376305_comment'></div>公讳纵。字希圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376305_comment'></div>太原祁人也。曾祖某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376305_comment'></div>誉合贵游。迹追<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1376305", 1376305, "Clauses/41/Comments/0")'>高矩</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376305_comment'></div>冥鸿不失。天爵逾优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376305_comment'></div>祖勖。皇任潭州端氏县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376305_comment'></div>价重儒林。行熟士范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376305_comment'></div>早推仁于宰字。巳属望于公台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376305_comment'></div>父载。皇任检校秘书少监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376305_comment'></div>赠少卿。早振宏猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376305_comment'></div>雅多奇节。自激封侯之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376305_comment'></div>欲垂济代之名。位郁于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376305_comment'></div>庆延其后。宜钟秀气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376305_comment'></div>历佐昌期。公幼挺英姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376305_comment'></div>夙彰杰操。镕金入用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376305_comment'></div>百汰唯精。建木标奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376305_comment'></div>千寻自植。禀说礼敦诗之教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376305_comment'></div>蕴经文纬武之材。欲绍家声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376305_comment'></div>遂参<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_35_1376305", 1376305, "Clauses/70/Comments/0")'>戎右</span>。研精玉帐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376305_comment'></div>演秘金韬。阴符必胜之机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376305_comment'></div>制于掌握。敌国相吞之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376305_comment'></div>决在毫釐。气盖三河声高六郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376305_comment'></div>长庆初以力战拜监察御史。名藩振迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376305_comment'></div>初加驭贵之荣。宪府扬威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376305_comment'></div>更帖承华之秩。太和九年授河中马步都知兵马使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376305_comment'></div>别选材官。教成骑阵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376305_comment'></div>自兹出讨。所向无前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376305_comment'></div>开成宰相郑公肃允属镇临。尤称<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_44_1376305", 1376305, "Clauses/89/Comments/0")'>鉴略</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376305_comment'></div>仰贤有素。授任不疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376305_comment'></div>擢奏马步都虞候。总中权之剧务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376305_comment'></div>示列国之上卿。喜动旌旗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376305_comment'></div>威生里巷。得人之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376305_comment'></div>他镇罕俦。会昌二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376305_comment'></div>武宗以回纥累叶凭骄。缘边<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_50_1376305", 1376305, "Clauses/101/Comments/0")'>扇酷</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1376305_comment'></div>久定扫平之计。尤难将领之权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1376305_comment'></div>既而蒲帅石公雄授命濯征。总戎出塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1376305_comment'></div>公为都知兵马使。捐家誓报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1376305_comment'></div>蓄锐别营。虏阵犹坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1376305_comment'></div>军锋稍壮。未振鼓行之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1376305_comment'></div>空稽庙算之筹。公内决一奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1376305_comment'></div>中分千骑。出徒间道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1376305_comment'></div>击若疾雷。巳继捷书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1376305_comment'></div>方麾大旆。岂俟排山之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1376305_comment'></div>乃成破竹之资。火烈风驱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1376305_comment'></div>震天骇地。血滂大漠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1376305_comment'></div>则澒洞倾河。颅积高山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1376305_comment'></div>则亘连绝塞。单于倾种。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1376305_comment'></div>贵主还都。克宣宗社之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1376305_comment'></div>顿雪人祇之愤。腥膻尽涤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1376305_comment'></div>氛祲皆消。万里长城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1376305_comment'></div>允膺朝寄。九重高枕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1376305_comment'></div>永殄国难。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_68_1376305", 1376305, "Clauses/137/Comments/0")'>秕糠</span>麟阁之雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1376305_comment'></div>孰为上将。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_69_1376305", 1376305, "Clauses/139/Comments/0")'>赞颂</span>龙庭之绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1376305_comment'></div>彼独何人。上乃遣中贵人刘英侔赍诏慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1376305_comment'></div>劳。自殿中侍御史超拜兼御史中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1376305_comment'></div>太尉李公久秉大权。素无滥赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1376305_comment'></div>倘非公论。莫致骤迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1376305_comment'></div>又拜晋州司马。上党兴祅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1376305_comment'></div>复提王旅。太原<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_75_1376305", 1376305, "Clauses/151/Comments/0")'>崇乱</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1376305_comment'></div>兼领郡符。授沁州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1376305_comment'></div>外训骁雄。内苏疲瘵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1376305_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_78_1376305", 1376305, "Clauses/156/Comments/0")'>殊庸</span>既显。善政亦闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1376305_comment'></div>擢邢州刺史充本州团练使。山东叛命积年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1376305_comment'></div>人为难理。公揣情设教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1376305_comment'></div>俗乃骤移。礼让既行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1376305_comment'></div>闾里相勉。旋当谢疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1376305_comment'></div>莫遂乞留。骥路未伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1376305_comment'></div>雀罗无愠。志讵忘于忧鲁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1376305_comment'></div>言恐及于平吴。久之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1376305_comment'></div>拜右龙武将军。仍知事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1376305_comment'></div>环翼宸居。佥谐宿德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1376305_comment'></div>刬烦苛于积弊。罢浮堕于窜名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1376305_comment'></div>心膂所资。貔貅自肃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1376305_comment'></div>虽居中而持重。每急病而让夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1376305_comment'></div>宣宗皇帝以河陇陷戎。祖宗遗愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1376305_comment'></div>将谋恢复。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_92_1376305", 1376305, "Clauses/185/Comments/0")'>翘注</span>忠贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1376305_comment'></div>又属盐州守臣政失人和。衅连羌部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1376305_comment'></div>雅重专城之选。仍当错节之难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1376305_comment'></div>公简在宸衷。对于便殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1376305_comment'></div>伏波强记。备述山川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1376305_comment'></div>充国勇行。请图方略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1376305_comment'></div>仍授盐州防御使检校常侍。凋残之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1376305_comment'></div>辑睦维艰。虏交未固于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_99_1376305", 1376305, "Clauses/199/Comments/0")'>解仇</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1376305_comment'></div>汉爵已颁于款塞。兵农竞劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1376305_comment'></div>夷夏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_101_1376305", 1376305, "Clauses/202/Comments/0")'>肃齐</span>。既而间使行边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1376305_comment'></div>飞章言状。上乃临轩叹激。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1376305_comment'></div>累诏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_103_1376305", 1376305, "Clauses/206/Comments/0")'>褒扬</span>。独授中规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1376305_comment'></div>希其重任。缮鲁州之坚垒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1376305_comment'></div>食力兼储。资陇右之威声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1376305_comment'></div>墟郊渐辟。和薰犷俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1376305_comment'></div>惠洽茕婺。已彰拓境之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1376305_comment'></div>即议疏封之赏。方延渥泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1376305_comment'></div>别立雄藩。而运郁时来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1376305_comment'></div>福亏冥报。连中峰而岳裂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1376305_comment'></div>袭右将以星沈。色惨朝端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1376305_comment'></div>悼深宸极。虽荆州罢市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1376305_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_113_1376305", 1376305, "Clauses/226/Comments/0")'>衡纪</span>屡迁。而蜀郡奉祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1376305_comment'></div>歌谣未息。古之遗爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1376305_comment'></div>无以加焉。咸通三年三月三日薨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1376305_comment'></div>享年六十八。理命具存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1376305_comment'></div>忧边是切。益励凿楹之诫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1376305_comment'></div>如传镂鼎之勋。某月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1376305_comment'></div>迁窆于某处。附先茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1376305_comment'></div>礼也。地启佳城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1376305_comment'></div>仪陈诏葬。舞鹤既占于形势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1376305_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_122_1376305", 1376305, "Clauses/244/Comments/0")'>谋龟</span>乃兆于公侯。封树增严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1376305_comment'></div>音容如在。皆知世祀之必昌矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1376305_comment'></div>初大理府君娶于陇西李氏。追赠陇西郡太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1376305_comment'></div>簪组联华。蘋蘩颂美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1376305_comment'></div>公实为嫡嗣。娶某郡石氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1376305_comment'></div>今封祁国太夫人。四德兼崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1376305_comment'></div>六姻推敬。早贻芳于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_128_1376305", 1376305, "Clauses/257/Comments/0")'>闺范</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1376305_comment'></div>宜应祷于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_129_1376305", 1376305, "Clauses/258/Comments/0")'>河灵</span>。保是钟祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1376305_comment'></div>成其鼎贵。五子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1376305_comment'></div>长曰重章。少称豪爽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1376305_comment'></div>深究韬钤。从击匈奴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1376305_comment'></div>著劳盟府。历诸卫将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1376305_comment'></div>终威州刺史。次曰重简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1376305_comment'></div>今任华州防御使检校兵马尚书。朗拔逸群。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1376305_comment'></div>惠和得众。左凭致捷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1376305_comment'></div>宏略居多。次曰重盈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1376305_comment'></div>今任陕虢观察使检校左仆射。沈几中济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1376305_comment'></div>雅量外夷。抚宁西河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1376305_comment'></div>镇静东道。次曰重荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1376305_comment'></div>今任河中节度使平章事。明澄海镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1376305_comment'></div>响震霜钟。体先觉以通奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1376305_comment'></div>应旁求而聘绩。锱铢王佐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1376305_comment'></div>表映人宗。自北府初援副车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1376305_comment'></div>即持戎律。外师谋入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1376305_comment'></div>危城势摇。四邻闭境以相观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1376305_comment'></div>一柱中天而独立。首排群议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1376305_comment'></div>决策勤王。赈赡诸郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1376305_comment'></div>指挥突将。破连营以通西路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1376305_comment'></div>质季弟而抚北军。同华既平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1376305_comment'></div>关防尽辟。继纳归明之众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1376305_comment'></div>遽成克复之功。羁制奸豪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1376305_comment'></div>保安封守。而又处劳期逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1376305_comment'></div>推俸僦徒。环筑解城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1376305_comment'></div>峻增关垒。举无遗策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1376305_comment'></div>动必中机。巨极底宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1376305_comment'></div>议勋殊等。次曰重益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1376305_comment'></div>勇而知义。和以秉谦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1376305_comment'></div>履险不疑。输忠必竭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1376305_comment'></div>以任子拜左千牛卫将军。初先公之捐馆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1376305_comment'></div>清尘未远。俭节弥彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1376305_comment'></div>产薄一廛。家徒四壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1376305_comment'></div>太夫人保和安遗。演训择邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1376305_comment'></div>俾蹈前修。皆能耸搆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1376305_comment'></div>且及亲之贵。自古罕兼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1376305_comment'></div>老莱则空耀彩衣。多惭绂冕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1376305_comment'></div>潘岳则唯称寿酒。固乏鼎彝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1376305_comment'></div>岂同大国进封。高堂拜庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1376305_comment'></div>刘加二骥。荀并八龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1376305_comment'></div>相印师坛。共观昼锦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1376305_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_171_1376305", 1376305, "Clauses/342/Comments/0")'>金相玉映</span>。各炫晨葩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1376305_comment'></div>犹陈断织之规。宁轸倚门之念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1376305_comment'></div>一女早适温氏。致克和于乡族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1376305_comment'></div>亦秉教于母仪。而又慈训诸孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1376305_comment'></div>蔚为令器。亦升宠秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1376305_comment'></div>森列庭闱。方传带励之盟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1376305_comment'></div>实冠古今之盛。夫力攘大患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1376305_comment'></div>显致阴功。则必降祐上元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1376305_comment'></div>绍熙来裔。永夷坚敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1376305_comment'></div>累洽仁风。果培树善之基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1376305_comment'></div>益遵胜残之报。司徒相公以丰功继志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1376305_comment'></div>异政传芳。褒崇致感于漏泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1376305_comment'></div>纪述欲先于表道。谋刊懿烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1376305_comment'></div>辱命芜词。合伸起敬之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1376305_comment'></div>敢避非才之诮。窃以祥浑流裔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1376305_comment'></div>文武争驱。家牒虽分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1376305_comment'></div>灵根共贯。至公崇上宰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1376305_comment'></div>绩赞中兴。彼江右之蝉联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1376305_comment'></div>昔惭<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_189_1376305", 1376305, "Clauses/378/Comments/0")'>丕运</span>。我晋阳之龟组。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1376305_comment'></div>今焕盛时。绵祚层澜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1376305_comment'></div>盍雕丰砥。铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1376305_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_192_1376305'>维德有融。维贤克嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1376305_comment'></div>礼法贻誉。勋华命瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1376305_comment'></div>杂蹑芳尘。纷纶宝气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1376305_comment'></div>武烈披显。儒风横被。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1376305_comment'></div>绩茂佐秦。名高辅魏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1376305_comment'></div>继祖无忝。图徽罔坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1376305_comment'></div>天临我唐。瑞降文昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1376305_comment'></div>驱崦逸发。驾浪雄张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1376305_comment'></div>虹摅耀采。雷震飞铓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1376305_comment'></div>英标激俗。峻节凌霜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1376305_comment'></div>研奇制变。料敌摧强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1376305_comment'></div>量吞巨壑。威摄穷荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1376305_comment'></div>申命宝臣。允兹薄伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1376305_comment'></div>壮志逾励。沈谋独决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1376305_comment'></div>日逐偷魂。天骄浴血。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1376305_comment'></div>鱼宝窜鼎。蚁惧搜穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1376305_comment'></div>轒辒下碎。搀抢上决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1376305_comment'></div>利尽长驱。声棱有截。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1376305_comment'></div>我武惟扬。我伐用张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1376305_comment'></div>俾侯宠锡。谒帝休光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1376305_comment'></div>和如金石。著在旂常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1376305_comment'></div>内司环卫。外峻巨防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1376305_comment'></div>通班石室。进秩银珰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1376305_comment'></div>临机必断。视物如伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1376305_comment'></div>两地辑绥。五原惠爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1376305_comment'></div>御侮材难。开疆计大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1376305_comment'></div>日驻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_218_1376305", 1376305, "Clauses/436/Comments/0")'>麾戈</span>。云横出塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1376305_comment'></div>白虏迎降。青羌自溃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1376305_comment'></div>戒守益严。资储永赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1376305_comment'></div>转轴摧旃。扬旌委旆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1376305_comment'></div>祯融积庆。祚表垂仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1376305_comment'></div>绵休自远。启映维新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1376305_comment'></div>恭恭令嗣。济济良臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1376305_comment'></div>名藩重寄。畅毂文茵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1376305_comment'></div>门交华戟。地鼓洪钧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1376305_comment'></div>推忠致主。履孝荣亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1376305_comment'></div>润接灵长。胜资磅礡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1376305_comment'></div>此兆<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_229_1376305", 1376305, "Clauses/458/Comments/0")'>松阡</span>。昔图烟阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1376305_comment'></div>汉诏腾褒。夏卿荐渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1376305_comment'></div>林蔚逾繁。源深不涸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_231_1376305_comment'></div>刊尔将来。缅怀可作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_232_1376305_comment'></div>克济宠珍。永延懿铄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1376305_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_234_1376305_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=884&endYear=884')">884年</a>　图举办佛事十会斋，撰文。作品：《十会斋》《迎修十会斋》<div id='poem_1376271' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376271' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376271?labeling=true' target='_blank'>迎修十会斋文</a><span class='authorDate'>（884年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14662, "唐末", "司空图", "poem_title_1376271")'>司空图</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376271_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376271'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376271'>非才非圣。过泰过荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376271_comment'></div>一举高第。两朝美官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376271_comment'></div>遭乱离而脱祸。归乡里而获安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376271_comment'></div>门户粗成。簪缨免绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376271_comment'></div>四十八年已往。未省归心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376271_comment'></div>百千万劫常来。岂迷善道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376271_comment'></div>今终可保。止绝何伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376271_comment'></div>灾疾所萦。古今常理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376271_comment'></div>但虽勤忏悔。未去膻腥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376271_comment'></div>大宜均罪于鼓刀。小合误伤于失手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376271_comment'></div>况蚊䖟之类。屡有伤残。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376271_comment'></div>仆乘之劳。时加箠楚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376271_comment'></div>或存或没。若重若轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376271_comment'></div>并愿各遂逍遥。永祛冤结。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376271_comment'></div>目前眷属。世世相逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376271_comment'></div>身后林泉。生生自适。<div class='inline' class='inlineComment2'>（此诗又列于郑谷名下，只能以“互见”方式处理。）</span>《〈月下留丹灶〉序》<div id='poem_12079' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_12079' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/12079?labeling=true' target='_blank'>月下留丹灶</a><span class='authorDate'>（887年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14662, "唐末", "司空图", "poem_title_12079")'>司空图</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_12079_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_12079'>有序：诗题五字，乃真仙之词也。邵阳某县人，或闻其山实异，斋祷积稔，果有蹈空而至者，涉笔附楹，久之，乃罢去。既而熟视木文，则字皆隐起成列矣。某年中，廉帅上闻，且命镵其逸迹，藏于郡廨，其后为刺史李岫所得。今传于君孙，岂精契之所感致耶？光启三年秋八月既望，愚获睹于王官别业。噫！迹虽显奇，道必体正，故为物怪之所中者，见之莫不洗然，欲盖其事，目击可数也。吾知挟邪佞以冒进者，亦当胆慄自废，岂俟图鼎燬犀而后辨奸妖之诡态哉！缀之全篇，以志诚敬，且期自警。泗水司空氏记。</div><div id='poem_preface_12079_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_12079'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_12079'>月下留丹灶，坛边树羽衣。<div id='poem_sentence_0_12079_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_12079'>异香人不觉，残夜鹤分飞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_12079_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>妖魅</span>敢扬威。<div id='poem_sentence_3_12079_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_12079'></div><div class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376275' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376275?labeling=true' target='_blank'>观音赞<span class='inlineComment2'>（證因亭并序）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（887年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14662, "唐末", "司空图", "poem_title_1376275")'>司空图</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1376275_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1376275'>万仞峨山之险。争竦祸梯。一坑浮世之尘。长遮觉路。骋云汉而贪味。临鼎镬以求哀。当种善缘。方希慈极。某早坚信受。频致感通。梦则可徵。足见未萌之诫。行而必禀。冀无入晨之虞。用建虔诚。永贻来裔。赞云。</div><div id='poem_preface_1376275_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376258' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376258?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送草书僧归楚越</a><span class='authorDate'>（897年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14662, "唐末", "司空图", "poem_title_1376258")'>司空图</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376258_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376258'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376258'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1376258", 1376258, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>伧荒</span>之俗。尤恶伎于文墨者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376258_comment'></div>华民流寓而至。则遽发其橐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376258_comment'></div>焚弃札牍之累以快。既自容矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376258_comment'></div>又仇沮继至者。若不胜其怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376258_comment'></div>噫。是华舌夷心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376258_comment'></div>而又甚之者矣。洎天下将乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376258_comment'></div>则虽吾里。其风亦变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376258_comment'></div>果<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1376258", 1376258, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>伧荒</span>之流民亦多矣。倘或未化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376258_comment'></div>亦其益孤。不能<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1376258", 1376258, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>自振</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376258_comment'></div>苟闻志于吾伎。则必跃而游之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376258_comment'></div>矧踵门而勤请者耶。𧦬光僧生于东越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376258_comment'></div>虽幼落于佛。而学无不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376258_comment'></div>故逸迹<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1376258", 1376258, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>遒劲</span>之外。亦恣为歌诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376258_comment'></div>以导江湖沉郁之气。是佛首而儒其业者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376258_comment'></div>虽孟荀复生。岂拒之哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376258_comment'></div>今<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1376258", 1376258, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>系名</span>内殿。且为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1376258", 1376258, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>归荣</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376258_comment'></div>足以光于远矣。永嘉西岑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376258_comment'></div>康乐胜游之最。是行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376258_comment'></div>为我以论诗一篇。题于绝壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376258_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_11854_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_11855' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_11855' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/11855?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_11855'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_11855'>衰鬓闲生少，丹梯望觉危。<div id='poem_sentence_0_11855_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_11855_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_11856' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_11856' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/11856?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_11856'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_11856'>落叶频惊鹿，连峰欲映雕。<div id='poem_sentence_0_11856_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_11856'>此生<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_11856", 11856, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>诗病</span>苦，此病更萧条。<div id='poem_sentence_1_11856_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_11856'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_11856_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_11857' class='authorDate'>（903年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_11859_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_11859'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_11859_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_11859'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_11859_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_11860' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_11860' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/11860?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其九 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（903年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_11860_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_11860'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_11860'>幽鸟穿篱去，邻翁采药回。<div id='poem_sentence_0_11860_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_11860'>云从潭底出，花向佛前开。<div id='poem_sentence_1_11860_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_11860'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_11860_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=903&endYear=903')">903年7月</a>　图在王官谷别业，修葺“休休亭”，撰文，自号耐辱居士。作品：《休休亭记》<div id='poem_1376260' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376260' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376260?labeling=true' target='_blank'>休休亭记</a><span class='authorDate'>（903年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14662, "唐末", "司空图", "poem_title_1376260")'>司空图</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376260_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376260'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376260'>休。休也美也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376260_comment'></div>既休而且美在焉。司空氏王官谷休休亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376260_comment'></div>本濯缨也。濯缨为陕军所焚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376260_comment'></div>愚<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1376260", 1376260, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>窜避</span>踰纪。天复癸亥岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376260_comment'></div>蒲稔人安。既归葺于坏垣之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376260_comment'></div>构不盈丈。然遽更其名者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376260_comment'></div>非以为奇。盖量其材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376260_comment'></div>一宜休也。揣其分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376260_comment'></div>二宜休也。且耄而瞆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376260_comment'></div>三宜休也。而又少而惰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376260_comment'></div>长而率。老而迂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376260_comment'></div>是三者。皆非救时之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376260_comment'></div>又宜休也。尚虑多难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376260_comment'></div>不能自信。既而昼寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376260_comment'></div>遇二僧。其名皆上方刻石者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376260_comment'></div>其一曰闉顽。谓吾曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376260_comment'></div>吾尝为汝之师也。汝昔矫于道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376260_comment'></div>锐而不固。为利欲之所拘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376260_comment'></div>幸悟而悔。将复从我于是溪耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376260_comment'></div>且汝虽退。亦尝为匪人之所嫉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376260_comment'></div>宜以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1376260", 1376260, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>耐辱</span>自警。庶保其终始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376260_comment'></div>与靖节醉吟第其品级于千载之下。复何求哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376260_comment'></div>因为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1376260", 1376260, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>耐辱</span>居士歌。题于亭之东北楹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376260_comment'></div>自开成丁巳岁七月。距今以是岁是月作是歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376260_comment'></div>亦乐天作传之年。六十七矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376260_comment'></div>休休乎。且又殁而可以自任者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376260_comment'></div>不增愧负于国家矣。复何求哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376260_comment'></div>天复癸亥秋七月二十七日。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1376260", 1376260, "Clauses/55/Comments/0")'>耐辱</span>居士司空图记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376260_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1376260_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=904&endYear=904')">904年</a>　此年为图一生所过的第二个甲子年。有诗。作品：《元日》<div id='poem_11783' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_11783' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/11783?labeling=true' target='_blank'>元日</a><span class='authorDate'>（904年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14662, "唐末", "司空图", "poem_title_11783")'>司空图</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_11783_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_11783'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_11783'>甲子今重数，生涯只自怜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_11783_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_11783'>殷勤元日日，欹午又明年。<div id='poem_sentence_1_11783_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_11783'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_11783_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=904&endYear=904')">904年</a>　图有文。作品：《与李生论诗书》<div id='poem_1376250' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376250' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376250?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与李生论诗书</a><span class='authorDate'>（904年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14662, "唐末", "司空图", "poem_title_1376250")'>司空图</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376250_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376250'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376250'>文之难而诗尤难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376250_comment'></div>古今之喻多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376250_comment'></div>愚以为辨于味而后可以言诗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376250_comment'></div>江岭之南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376250_comment'></div>凡足资于适口者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376250_comment'></div>若醯非不酸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376250_comment'></div>止于酸而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376250_comment'></div>若鹾非不咸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376250_comment'></div>止于咸而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376250_comment'></div>中华之人所以充饥而遽辍者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376250_comment'></div>知其咸酸之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376250_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1376250", 1376250, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>醇美</span>者有所乏耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376250_comment'></div>彼江岭之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376250_comment'></div>习之而不辨也宜哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376250_comment'></div>诗贯六义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376250_comment'></div>则讽谕抑扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376250_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1376250", 1376250, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>渟蓄</span>渊雅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376250_comment'></div>皆在其中矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376250_comment'></div>然直致所得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376250_comment'></div>以格自奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376250_comment'></div>前辈诸集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376250_comment'></div>亦不专工于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376250_comment'></div>矧其下者耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376250_comment'></div>王右丞韦苏州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376250_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1376250", 1376250, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>澄澹</span>精致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376250_comment'></div>格在其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376250_comment'></div>岂妨于道学哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376250_comment'></div>贾阆仙诚有警句。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376250_comment'></div>然视其全篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376250_comment'></div>意思殊馁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376250_comment'></div>大抵附于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_1376250", 1376250, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>蹇涩</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376250_comment'></div>方可致才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376250_comment'></div>亦为体之不备也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376250_comment'></div>矧其下者哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376250_comment'></div>噫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376250_comment'></div>近而不浮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376250_comment'></div>远而不尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376250_comment'></div>然后可以言韵外之致耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376250_comment'></div>愚窃尝自负。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376250_comment'></div>既久而愈觉然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376250_comment'></div>然得于早春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376250_comment'></div>则有草嫩侵沙长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376250_comment'></div>冰轻著雨销。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376250_comment'></div>又人家寒食月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376250_comment'></div>花影午时天<span class='inlineComment2'>（上句云隔谷见鸡犬山苗接楚田）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376250_comment'></div>又雨微吟足思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376250_comment'></div>花落梦无憀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376250_comment'></div>又夜短猿悲减。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376250_comment'></div>风和鹊喜灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376250_comment'></div>得于山中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376250_comment'></div>则有坡暖冬生笋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1376250_comment'></div>松凉夏健人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1376250_comment'></div>又川明虹照雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1376250_comment'></div>树密鸟冲人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1376250_comment'></div>得于江南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1376250_comment'></div>则有日带潮声晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1376250_comment'></div>烟和楚色秋<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作戍鼓和潮暗船灯照岛幽本集同）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1376250_comment'></div>又曲塘春尽雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1376250_comment'></div>方响夜深船。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1376250_comment'></div>得于塞上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1376250_comment'></div>则有马色经寒惨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1376250_comment'></div>雕声带晚饥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1376250_comment'></div>得于丧乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1376250_comment'></div>则有骅骝思故第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1376250_comment'></div>鹦鹉失佳人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1376250_comment'></div>又鲸鲵人海涸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1376250_comment'></div>魑魅棘林幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1376250_comment'></div>得于道官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1376250_comment'></div>则有棋声花院闭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1376250_comment'></div>幡影石坛高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1376250_comment'></div>得于夏景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1376250_comment'></div>则有地凉清鹤梦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1376250_comment'></div>林静肃僧仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1376250_comment'></div>得于佛寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1376250_comment'></div>则有松日明金像。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1376250_comment'></div>苔龛响木鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1376250_comment'></div>又解吟僧亦俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1376250_comment'></div>爱舞鹤终卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1376250_comment'></div>得于郊园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1376250_comment'></div>则有暖景鸡声美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1376250_comment'></div>微风蝶影繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1376250_comment'></div>又远陂春早渗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1376250_comment'></div>犹有水禽飞<span class='inlineComment2'>（上句云绿树连村暗黄花入麦稀）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1376250_comment'></div>得于乐府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1376250_comment'></div>则有晚妆留拜月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1376250_comment'></div>春睡更生香。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1376250_comment'></div>得于寂寥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1376250_comment'></div>则有孤萤出荒池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1376250_comment'></div>落叶穿破屋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1376250_comment'></div>得于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_89_1376250", 1376250, "Clauses/89/Comments/0")'>惬适</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1376250_comment'></div>则有客来当意惬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1376250_comment'></div>花发遇歌成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1376250_comment'></div>虽庶几不滨于浅涸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1376250_comment'></div>亦未废作者之讥诃也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1376250_comment'></div>七言云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1376250_comment'></div>逃难人多分隙地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1376250_comment'></div>放生鹿大出寒林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1376250_comment'></div>又得剑乍如添健仆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1376250_comment'></div>亡书久似忆良朋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1376250_comment'></div>又孤屿池痕春涨满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1376250_comment'></div>小栏花韵午晴初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1376250_comment'></div>又五更惆怅回孤枕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1376250_comment'></div>犹自残灯照落花<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1376250_comment'></div>又殷勤元旦日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1376250_comment'></div>欹午又明年<span class='inlineComment2'>（上句云甲子今重数生涯只自怜）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1376250_comment'></div>皆不拘于一概也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1376250_comment'></div>盖绝句之作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1376250_comment'></div>本于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_107_1376250", 1376250, "Clauses/107/Comments/0")'>诣极</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1376250_comment'></div>此外<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_108_1376250", 1376250, "Clauses/108/Comments/0")'>千变万状</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1376250_comment'></div>不知所以神而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_109_1376250", 1376250, "Clauses/109/Comments/0")'>自神</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1376250_comment'></div>岂容易哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1376250_comment'></div>足下之诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1376250_comment'></div>时辈固有难色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1376250_comment'></div>傥复以全美为上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1376250_comment'></div>即知味外之旨矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1376250_comment'></div>勉旃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1376250_comment'></div>司空表圣再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_116_1376250_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1376250'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_102_1376250_0'>⑴ 上句云故国春归未有涯小楼栏槛别人家</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1376250_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=904&endYear=904')">904年</a>　年底将度岁，图有诗作。作品：《岁尽二首》<div id='poem_11817' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_11817' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14662, "唐末", "司空图", "poem_title_11817")'>司空图</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_11817_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_11817'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_11817'>明日添一岁，端忧奈尔何。<div id='poem_sentence_0_11817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_11817'>冲寒出洞口，犹校夕阳多。<div id='poem_sentence_1_11817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_11817'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_11817_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_11818' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_11818' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/11818?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_11818'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_11818'>莫话伤心事，投春满鬓霜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_11818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_11818'>殷勤共尊酒，今岁只残阳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_11818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_11818'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_11818_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=905&endYear=905')">905年1月7日</a>　图有诗作。作品：《乙丑人日》<div id='poem_11753' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_11753' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/11753?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乙丑人日</a><span class='authorDate'>（905年1月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14662, "唐末", "司空图", "poem_title_11753")'>司空图</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_11753_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_11753'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_11753'>自怪扶持七十身，归来又见故乡春。<div id='poem_sentence_0_11753_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_11753'>今朝人日逢人喜，不料<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_11753", 11753, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>偷生</span>作老人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_11753_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_11753'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_11753_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=905&endYear=905')">905年7月16日</a>　图撰《泽州灵泉院记》<div id='poem_1376264' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376264' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376264?labeling=true' target='_blank'>泽州灵泉院记</a><span class='authorDate'>（905年7月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14662, "唐末", "司空图", "poem_title_1376264")'>司空图</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376264_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376264'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376264'>严饬祠宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376264_comment'></div>非欲侈于自奉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376264_comment'></div>盖不崇不侈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376264_comment'></div>无以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1376264", 1376264, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>耸动</span>群品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376264_comment'></div>俾坚向善之心耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376264_comment'></div>况帝梦可徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376264_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1376264", 1376264, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>华缘</span>已熟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376264_comment'></div>山川神祗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376264_comment'></div>罔不荐款。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376264_comment'></div>故自京邑以及遐裔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376264_comment'></div>胜槩相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376264_comment'></div>皆奠厥居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376264_comment'></div>中条发于蒲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376264_comment'></div>趋于艮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376264_comment'></div>杰出而为太行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376264_comment'></div>则天坛不得不冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376264_comment'></div>盖华嵩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376264_comment'></div>争勍日观也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376264_comment'></div>其北川壑会流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376264_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1376264", 1376264, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>盘郁</span>粹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376264_comment'></div>自高平西顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376264_comment'></div>以至灵泉极矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376264_comment'></div>泉之为灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376264_comment'></div>非惟利物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376264_comment'></div>亦当<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1376264", 1376264, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>滋润</span>所及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376264_comment'></div>不育毒螫也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376264_comment'></div>其院东向<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1376264", 1376264, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>显豁</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376264_comment'></div>亘为大川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376264_comment'></div>端门洞辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376264_comment'></div>正与旭日相迓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376264_comment'></div>岂梵书所谓震旦者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376264_comment'></div>此其證哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376264_comment'></div>且有为无为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376264_comment'></div>于我不碍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376264_comment'></div>弛之则若涸其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376264_comment'></div>用之则必滂其外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376264_comment'></div>皆克固其源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376264_comment'></div>乃能动而必济也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376264_comment'></div>今禅宿洪密长老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376264_comment'></div>俗姓刘氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376264_comment'></div>本儒家子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376264_comment'></div>早诣石霜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376264_comment'></div>契其大旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376264_comment'></div>烦而不挠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376264_comment'></div>简而必周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376264_comment'></div>初自清凉历览至是山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376264_comment'></div>乃创<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_1376264", 1376264, "Clauses/46/Comments/0")'>林栖</span>之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376264_comment'></div>遇太尉李公驻军高平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376264_comment'></div>首资葺构。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376264_comment'></div>远近道俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376264_comment'></div>莫不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_50_1376264", 1376264, "Clauses/50/Comments/0")'>归向</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1376264_comment'></div>今蒲芮陇西左揆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1376264_comment'></div>常因题纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1376264_comment'></div>亦备赞扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1376264_comment'></div>则密公之道益光矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1376264_comment'></div>凡制经楼斋堂共一百馀间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1376264_comment'></div>又塑罗汉洁刻之相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1376264_comment'></div>以渐化服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1376264_comment'></div>而后日集方丈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1376264_comment'></div>敷演上乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1376264_comment'></div>自江汉北渡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1376264_comment'></div>以至魏晋之交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1376264_comment'></div>其俗坚悍难诱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1376264_comment'></div>今则悉为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_63_1376264", 1376264, "Clauses/63/Comments/0")'>佛人</span>矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1376264_comment'></div>且善教童孺者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1376264_comment'></div>虽指摘其书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1376264_comment'></div>而必以言反覆晓谕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1376264_comment'></div>当自释然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1376264_comment'></div>若典教积于前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1376264_comment'></div>笞挞骇于侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1376264_comment'></div>彼将<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_70_1376264", 1376264, "Clauses/70/Comments/0")'>窜匿</span>之不暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1376264_comment'></div>讵肯说而从命哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1376264_comment'></div>律刑书也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1376264_comment'></div>经诰誓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1376264_comment'></div>禅乃诱劝之宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1376264_comment'></div>先驯其性而后入人者耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1376264_comment'></div>故其道至隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1376264_comment'></div>其功至博。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1376264_comment'></div>不可废也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1376264_comment'></div>常念畜役之外以逮<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_79_1376264", 1376264, "Clauses/79/Comments/0")'>佣隶</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1376264_comment'></div>虽豢养至丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1376264_comment'></div>莫不苦于受制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1376264_comment'></div>殊不知<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_82_1376264", 1376264, "Clauses/82/Comments/0")'>羁鞅</span>之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1376264_comment'></div>或能<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_83_1376264", 1376264, "Clauses/83/Comments/0")'>避免</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1376264_comment'></div>而方寸之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1376264_comment'></div>不形不声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1376264_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_86_1376264", 1376264, "Clauses/86/Comments/0")'>牙孽</span>牢萌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1376264_comment'></div>托其力者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1376264_comment'></div>愈不能争。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1376264_comment'></div>以此沦陷死生之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1376264_comment'></div>绵劫不能自脱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1376264_comment'></div>其苦何如哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1376264_comment'></div>噫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1376264_comment'></div>苟非三世之尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1376264_comment'></div>夷山斡海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1376264_comment'></div>六祖亲授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1376264_comment'></div>捩其钳𮡧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1376264_comment'></div>长老继作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1376264_comment'></div>磨昏抉瞆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1376264_comment'></div>则彼爨膏镬而勇于自浴者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1376264_comment'></div>虽糜烂其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1376264_comment'></div>犹未悔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1376264_comment'></div>今乃聚其徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1376264_comment'></div>侈其居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1376264_comment'></div>永为一檀施之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1376264_comment'></div>且俾其福慧皆殖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1376264_comment'></div>然则密公之积。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1376264_comment'></div>焉可抑没哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1376264_comment'></div>耐辱居士病且死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1376264_comment'></div>不忍其门人慧依慧海之勤请也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1376264_comment'></div>直纪所行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1376264_comment'></div>惟以漏略为愧云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1376264_comment'></div>天祐二年岁次乙丑七月望日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_112_1376264_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=905&endYear=908')">905-908年</a>，69-72岁</div><div id='decc61d54cd1472c8aa53d7fa921781e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=905&endYear=905')">905年</a>　图脱柳璨之祸，回王官谷，有诗。作品：《丑年冬》<div id='poem_11781' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_11781' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/11781?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丑年冬</a><span class='authorDate'>（905年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript:
