-----title
西安
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='bf348d0f03864555a0ead9dcf9ddf3d2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bf348d0f03864555a0ead9dcf9ddf3d2");'><span id='bf348d0f03864555a0ead9dcf9ddf3d2_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=865&endYear=865')">865年</a>，29岁</div><div id='bf348d0f03864555a0ead9dcf9ddf3d2' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋，图当在京师长安准备参加进士科举。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>本年，图于科举前上书夏侯孜。作品：《上谯公书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（该书亦可能写于咸通九年，但以写于本年可能性更大，今暂系于本年。）</span><div id='poem_1376247' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376247' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376247?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上谯公书</a><span class='authorDate'>（865年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14662, "唐末", "司空图", "poem_title_1376247")'>司空图</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376247_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376247'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376247'>再拜。愚伏以布衣犯将相之威者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376247_comment'></div>近皆笑率指愚为狂。是轻薄子不能以恢然之量待今贤杰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376247_comment'></div>相公得不念之耶。某迹拘世累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376247_comment'></div>而业久于山。援古勘今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376247_comment'></div>思有所发者。盖窃惟近朝据重位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376247_comment'></div>而勇蹈功名之利。耻天下有遗才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376247_comment'></div>直吾相国也。又敢求吾相之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376247_comment'></div>所以未忍弃生民之望者。固非<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1376247", 1376247, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>濡濡</span>于富贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376247_comment'></div>岂不以时持大柄。事或阻心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376247_comment'></div>且后弛张。俾无遗恨于不朽耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376247_comment'></div>愚以是窃抃。有以企天下之福矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376247_comment'></div>虽在于至愚。犹有轻虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376247_comment'></div>诚以相公既当有得贤之盛。将尤有惜夫自持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376247_comment'></div>既尝独决机权。将尤以事不足问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376247_comment'></div>则党附之贤或兴。而专美之道可隘耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376247_comment'></div>请陈其说。夫用人固得矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376247_comment'></div>亦在知失之不足盖为明。则伪者惩而实者劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376247_comment'></div>且无伤于爱士。处事也固济矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376247_comment'></div>又知谋之不必自我出为知。则听日广而神不劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376247_comment'></div>且无伤于好谋。是道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376247_comment'></div>盖贤哲用之而不竭。相公得之而不疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376247_comment'></div>坦怀至公。自无愧古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376247_comment'></div>然后文尚制科之选。武先西北之虞<span class='inlineComment2'>（前年已上书蜀相）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376247_comment'></div>抑<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1376247", 1376247, "Clauses/46/Comments/0")'>简诞</span>以捐空。峻规程而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1376247", 1376247, "Clauses/47/Comments/0")'>括实</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376247_comment'></div>则病应适时之宜尽矣。此皆相公夙自践于沉实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376247_comment'></div>而小子虽<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1376247", 1376247, "Clauses/50/Comments/0")'>吃悸</span>。不能<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1376247", 1376247, "Clauses/51/Comments/0")'>面发</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376247_comment'></div>愿激扬于片时耳。非为挟利之资也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376247_comment'></div>抑自古钓奇而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1376247", 1376247, "Clauses/54/Comments/0")'>售迹</span>者。既多以分蹇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376247_comment'></div>动无所合。且实必俟临机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376247_comment'></div>方见其万一。非敢<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1376247", 1376247, "Clauses/59/Comments/0")'>率易</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376247_comment'></div>并渎尊威。干犯之诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376247_comment'></div>则不复自同轻薄子以为疑惧。俟命再拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376247_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1376247_comment'></div></div></div><br id='poem_sentence_0_1376252_comment'></div>某赘于天地之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376252_comment'></div>三十三年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376252_comment'></div>及览古之贤豪事迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376252_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1376252", 1376252, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>惭企</span>不暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376252_comment'></div>则又环顾尘蔑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376252_comment'></div>自知不足为天下之赘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376252_comment'></div>噫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376252_comment'></div>岂非才不足而自强耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376252_comment'></div>虽然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376252_comment'></div>丈夫志业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376252_comment'></div>引之犹恐自跼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376252_comment'></div>诚不敢以此为惮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376252_comment'></div>故文之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376252_comment'></div>往探治乱之本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376252_comment'></div>俟知我者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376252_comment'></div>纵其狂愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376252_comment'></div>以成万一之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376252_comment'></div>壮心未决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376252_comment'></div>俯仰人郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376252_comment'></div>今遇先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376252_comment'></div>俾仆得以尽论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376252_comment'></div>愿修讨源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376252_comment'></div>然后次第及于济时之机也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376252_comment'></div>唐虞之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376252_comment'></div>三代非不敝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376252_comment'></div>赖圣人先其极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376252_comment'></div>而变之不滞耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376252_comment'></div>秦汉而下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376252_comment'></div>时风益浇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376252_comment'></div>视之而不知其弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376252_comment'></div>矫之而不知其变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376252_comment'></div>文质莫辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376252_comment'></div>法制失中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376252_comment'></div>侮儒必止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376252_comment'></div>沈儒必削。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376252_comment'></div>则士大夫虽有自负雅道者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376252_comment'></div>既不足以振之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376252_comment'></div>而又激时之怨耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376252_comment'></div>汉魏之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376252_comment'></div>其弊盖极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376252_comment'></div>惩马融胡广之流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376252_comment'></div>故李膺质而峻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376252_comment'></div>诫何晏桓范之俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376252_comment'></div>则王衍简而清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376252_comment'></div>矫之而不和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376252_comment'></div>滞之而不顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376252_comment'></div>始以类聚相扇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376252_comment'></div>终以浮党见嫉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376252_comment'></div>而至家国皆瘁而不寤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376252_comment'></div>悲夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1376252_comment'></div>故愚以为今欲应时之病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1376252_comment'></div>即莫若尚通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1376252_comment'></div>不必叛道而攻利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1376252_comment'></div>隘则驱之以仇已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1376252_comment'></div>树政之基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1376252_comment'></div>莫若尚法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1376252_comment'></div>不必任察而嗜刑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1376252_comment'></div>弛则怠之以陷人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1376252_comment'></div>舍此二者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1376252_comment'></div>伊周不能为当今之治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1376252_comment'></div>苟在位者有问于愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1376252_comment'></div>必先存质以究实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1376252_comment'></div>镇浮而劝用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1376252_comment'></div>使天下知有所竟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1376252_comment'></div>而不自窘以罪时焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1376252_comment'></div>噫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1376252_comment'></div>有必不能辨之于言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1376252_comment'></div>有之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1376252_comment'></div>未有无其心无其言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1376252_comment'></div>可以垂名于不朽者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1376252_comment'></div>且一家之治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1376252_comment'></div>我是而未必皆行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1376252_comment'></div>一国之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1376252_comment'></div>我公而未必皆行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1376252_comment'></div>就其间量可为而为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1376252_comment'></div>当有以及于物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1376252_comment'></div>不可为而不为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1376252_comment'></div>亦足以见其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1376252_comment'></div>必曰俟时而后济其仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1376252_comment'></div>盖无心之论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1376252_comment'></div>夫百人并迫于水火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1376252_comment'></div>可皆救之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1376252_comment'></div>斯为幸矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1376252_comment'></div>不可皆救。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1376252_comment'></div>则将竭力救其一二耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1376252_comment'></div>亦将高拱以视之耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1376252_comment'></div>幸先生以质于时贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1376252_comment'></div>审其有心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1376252_comment'></div>然后可为编次第之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1376252_comment'></div>再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_90_1376252_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_15_1376286_comment'></div>紫坛殷荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376286_comment'></div>受繁祉以贻休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376286_comment'></div>备缉化之元机。<div id='poem_sentence_31_1376286_comment'></div>龙蹲丧味。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376286_comment'></div>超浩叹以违齐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376286_comment'></div>而大朴久雕。<div id='poem_sentence_99_1376286_comment'></div>斗轻盈而入玩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1376286_comment'></div>逞夷冶以乘春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1376286_comment'></div>名编协律之籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1376286_comment'></div>妙轶总章之观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1376286_comment'></div>元云起唱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1376286_comment'></div>绛树分行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1376286_comment'></div>法婴之暂赏人间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1376286_comment'></div>净婉之曾誇掌上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1376286_comment'></div>翠娥低敛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1376286_comment'></div>儗画扇而初疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1376286_comment'></div>凤翼旋披。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1376286_comment'></div>蹑染香而不印。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1376286_comment'></div>绿萝山畔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1376286_comment'></div>徒有传名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1376286_comment'></div>金谷楼中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1376286_comment'></div>犹应掩嫭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1376286_comment'></div>轻埃渐弭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1376286_comment'></div>泛空碧之横云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1376286_comment'></div>曳绪黎收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1376286_comment'></div>失<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_119_1376286", 1376286, "Clauses/119/Comments/0")'>凌波</span>之回雪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1376286_comment'></div>既而麟麛罢飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1376286_comment'></div>龙辔倾夕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1376286_comment'></div>簇红艳于金擎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1376286_comment'></div>滟兰英于琥珀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1376286_comment'></div>瑶钗递约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1376286_comment'></div>粉镜齐匀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1376286_comment'></div>炫<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_126_1376286", 1376286, "Clauses/126/Comments/0")'>华藻</span>之新装。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1376286_comment'></div>捧重霄之宝器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1376286_comment'></div>凄锵缥缈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1376286_comment'></div>轻飔渐拂于花丛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1376286_comment'></div>鸳鹄和鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1376286_comment'></div>上客潜惊于烟隥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1376286_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_132_1376286", 1376286, "Clauses/132/Comments/0")'>雕筵</span>让促。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1376286_comment'></div>玉斝横飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1376286_comment'></div>堕珥颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1376286_comment'></div>牵裾屡舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1376286_comment'></div>笺霏彩笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1376286_comment'></div>递申燕婉之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1376286_comment'></div>月晓莲塘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1376286_comment'></div>更乱鸡人之唱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1376286_comment'></div>必使倾欢买笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1376286_comment'></div>怅归路于太行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1376286_comment'></div>失意沉情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1376286_comment'></div>怜霜锋于使客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1376286_comment'></div>且秦图启霸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1376286_comment'></div>先输婵媛之工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1376286_comment'></div>楚剑宣铓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1376286_comment'></div>宁谢优倡之拙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1376286_comment'></div>龟山远蔽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1376286_comment'></div>迷津则元类<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_149_1376286", 1376286, "Clauses/149/Comments/0")'>吹毛</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1376286_comment'></div>鱼藻陈规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1376286_comment'></div>式宴则唯思在镐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1376286_comment'></div>繁华托好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1376286_comment'></div>沦误忘归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1376286_comment'></div>盛德何观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1376286_comment'></div>雅风洞丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1376286_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_156_1376286", 1376286, "Clauses/156/Comments/0")'>愉心</span>炫目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1376286_comment'></div>俱谋越礼之讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1376286_comment'></div>异轸分流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1376286_comment'></div>弥会相淫之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1376286_comment'></div>犹是史迁<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_160_1376286", 1376286, "Clauses/160/Comments/0")'>衔涕</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1376286_comment'></div>愤沉湎于衰周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1376286_comment'></div>荀勖披丹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1376286_comment'></div>愿仪形于治古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1376286_comment'></div>乃曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1376286_comment'></div>升下含微握契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1376286_comment'></div>映调露之微踪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1376286_comment'></div>驭道斯元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1376286_comment'></div>演咸池之积润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1376286_comment'></div>双龙肃驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1376286_comment'></div>爰钦九辩之神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1376286_comment'></div>八凤迎祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1376286_comment'></div>再袭五英之荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1376286_comment'></div>非烟毓媚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1376286_comment'></div>应玉烛以登歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1376286_comment'></div>皓质依仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1376286_comment'></div>乐神扃而畅律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1376286_comment'></div>虽循机之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1376286_comment'></div>必无谢于继韶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1376286_comment'></div>而制俗之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1376286_comment'></div>犹未先于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_180_1376286", 1376286, "Clauses/180/Comments/0")'>放郑</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1376286_comment'></div>夫南薰北鄙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1376286_comment'></div>祸福相淫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1376286_comment'></div>感物穷微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1376286_comment'></div>兴亡是系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1376286_comment'></div>繁声罢奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1376286_comment'></div>建武之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_186_1376286", 1376286, "Clauses/186/Comments/0")'>贞范</span>斯存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1376286_comment'></div>妖玩无容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1376286_comment'></div>太初之芳尘可挹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1376286_comment'></div>得不翘襟酌训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1376286_comment'></div>经虑防奢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1376286_comment'></div>揖璇玑养命之符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1376286_comment'></div>受帝女昭华之琯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1376286_comment'></div>探灵测化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1376286_comment'></div>但<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_194_1376286", 1376286, "Clauses/194/Comments/0")'>累黍</span>而无差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1376286_comment'></div>思古妍幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1376286_comment'></div>将一夔而可任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1376286_comment'></div>悬衡睿旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1376286_comment'></div>合契乾心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1376286_comment'></div>追六代之英华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1376286_comment'></div>汰百王之荡涤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1376286_comment'></div>岂容苏夔席势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1376286_comment'></div>胶独见以邀能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1376286_comment'></div>高肇凭豪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1376286_comment'></div>抑群儒而徇已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1376286_comment'></div>变唯尚质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1376286_comment'></div>贵在<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_206_1376286", 1376286, "Clauses/206/Comments/0")'>扬清</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1376286_comment'></div>动以敷愉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1376286_comment'></div>绰之仁义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1376286_comment'></div>非<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_209_1376286", 1376286, "Clauses/209/Comments/0")'>简节繁文</span>之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1376286_comment'></div>不用于明庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1376286_comment'></div>非崇严<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_211_1376286", 1376286, "Clauses/211/Comments/0")'>煦育</span>之姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1376286_comment'></div>不传于委巷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1376286_comment'></div>使牛刀学制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1376286_comment'></div>必笺武邑之猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1376286_comment'></div>鹭羽将持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1376286_comment'></div>敢惧宛邱之刺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1376286_comment'></div>然后返歌莺于海峤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1376286_comment'></div>维舞骥于璜台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1376286_comment'></div>鱼龙息<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_219_1376286", 1376286, "Clauses/219/Comments/0")'>曼衍</span>之陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1376286_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_220_1376286", 1376286, "Clauses/220/Comments/0")'>鞮译</span>沮兜离之献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1376286_comment'></div>掖庭<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_221_1376286", 1376286, "Clauses/221/Comments/0")'>弦吹</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1376286_comment'></div>先罢赏于材人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1376286_comment'></div>司隶<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_223_1376286", 1376286, "Clauses/223/Comments/0")'>纠绳</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1376286_comment'></div>次申严于权右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1376286_comment'></div>傥莲舟帝子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1376286_comment'></div>独贻招隐之诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1376286_comment'></div>绮殿台臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1376286_comment'></div>别奏登封之颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1376286_comment'></div>酒唯洽礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1376286_comment'></div>遽无纵于流连。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1376286_comment'></div>乐则缘情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_231_1376286_comment'></div>但取优于名教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_232_1376286_comment'></div>俾春浓上苑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1376286_comment'></div>空凝桃李之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1376286_comment'></div>月满西园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1376286_comment'></div>寂寞芙蓉之艳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1376286_comment'></div>式敷围范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1376286_comment'></div>交畅人情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1376286_comment'></div>澄积乐于一时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_239_1376286_comment'></div>靡清风于四表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1376286_comment'></div>岂复平西长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_241_1376286_comment'></div>荐<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_242_1376286", 1376286, "Clauses/242/Comments/0")'>淑丽</span>以希恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_242_1376286_comment'></div>司律中郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_243_1376286_comment'></div>恣哇咬而被宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_244_1376286_comment'></div>则必三雍八佾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_245_1376286_comment'></div>休僭滥于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_246_1376286", 1376286, "Clauses/246/Comments/0")'>豪门</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_246_1376286_comment'></div>春诵夏弦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_247_1376286_comment'></div>服祇庸于冑子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_248_1376286_comment'></div>自然调元演庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_249_1376286_comment'></div>开瑞历而贯氛氲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_250_1376286_comment'></div>驾俗遗华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_251_1376286_comment'></div>抚鸿钧而明揖让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_252_1376286_comment'></div>臣业惭待扣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_253_1376286_comment'></div>恩谢识微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_254_1376286_comment'></div>鹿鸣传锦里之谣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_255_1376286_comment'></div>象舞阙青衿之致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_256_1376286_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_257_1376286", 1376286, "Clauses/257/Comments/0")'>孤桐</span>韬响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_257_1376286_comment'></div>唯均雨露之濡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_258_1376286_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_259_1376286", 1376286, "Clauses/259/Comments/0")'>泗石</span>含清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_259_1376286_comment'></div>未冠云韶之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_260_1376286_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_261_1376286", 1376286, "Clauses/261/Comments/0")'>编蓬</span>反素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_261_1376286_comment'></div>誓击壤以亡机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_262_1376286_comment'></div>汗简潜心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_263_1376286_comment'></div>警夺朱而发愤。<div id='poem_sentence_268_1376286_comment'></div>访徽猷于显庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_269_1376286_comment'></div>酌<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_270_1376286", 1376286, "Clauses/270/Comments/0")'>茂实</span>于开元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_270_1376286_comment'></div>坐镇浇讹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_271_1376286_comment'></div>式清缁蠹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_272_1376286_comment'></div>是用撤书竦志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_273_1376286_comment'></div>慕高允之贞规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_274_1376286_comment'></div>企日裁成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_275_1376286_comment'></div>继翁卿之谠议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_276_1376286_comment'></div>春台自煦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_277_1376286_comment'></div>舞希金奏之和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_278_1376286_comment'></div>下曲难投。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_279_1376286_comment'></div>犹阻钧天之荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_280_1376286_comment'></div>谕锦屏而托讽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_281_1376286_comment'></div>徒欲输忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_282_1376286_comment'></div>仰魏阙以兢魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_283_1376286_comment'></div>翻同滥窃。</div><div id='poem_sentence_284_1376286_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=880&endYear=880')">880年10—11月</a>　图约在十月十一月期间，编选友人诗作成集。作品：《擢英集》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此集今佚，仅存《擢英集》述。）</span><div id='poem_1376296' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376296' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376296?labeling=true' target='_blank'>擢英集述</a><span class='authorDate'>（880年10—11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14662, "唐末", "司空图", "poem_title_1376296")'>司空图</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376296_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376296'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376296'>名利之机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376296_comment'></div>古今相轧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376296_comment'></div>混惟一致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376296_comment'></div>宏则两忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376296_comment'></div>或高视于掞天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376296_comment'></div>或雄张于击水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376296_comment'></div>舍麟作凤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376296_comment'></div>孰降等夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376296_comment'></div>捐璧握珠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376296_comment'></div>自能辉映。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376296_comment'></div>遇则以身行道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376296_comment'></div>穷则见志于言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376296_comment'></div>各擅英灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376296_comment'></div>宁甘顿挫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376296_comment'></div>自昭明妙选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376296_comment'></div>振起斯文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376296_comment'></div>荣虽著于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1376296", 1376296, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>方将</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376296_comment'></div>恨皆缠于既往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376296_comment'></div>当西施之玩镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376296_comment'></div>不赏娥眉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376296_comment'></div>岂伯乐之停车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376296_comment'></div>空收骏骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376296_comment'></div>乃使盛时才子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376296_comment'></div>翻衔泣玉之冤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376296_comment'></div>异代沈魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376296_comment'></div>祇掷凌云之誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376296_comment'></div>九原谁诧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376296_comment'></div>千载徒悬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376296_comment'></div>思格前规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376296_comment'></div>用伸来者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376296_comment'></div>至若金犀照灼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376296_comment'></div>纨绮追攀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376296_comment'></div>裕之则管乐通期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376296_comment'></div>峻之则彭韩绝倒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376296_comment'></div>人人<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_34_1376296", 1376296, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>骥路</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376296_comment'></div>云台之此日豪华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376296_comment'></div>处处鸾丛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376296_comment'></div>仙馆则当时寥落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376296_comment'></div>各铭钟鼎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376296_comment'></div>竞焕缇油。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376296_comment'></div>耻发誉于雕虫。<div id='poem_sentence_42_1376296_comment'></div>纵阻争先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376296_comment'></div>机中之五色烟霞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376296_comment'></div>无妨倍价。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376296_comment'></div>知音嘿已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376296_comment'></div>作者谁尤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376296_comment'></div>用徵逸藻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376296_comment'></div>想其黎黄洞奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1376296_comment'></div>锦绣毕陈。<div id='poem_sentence_59_1376296_comment'></div>欣传赏奏之徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1376296_comment'></div>免茹投光之叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1376296_comment'></div>固已翘心不朽。<div id='poem_sentence_64_1376296_comment'></div>炫采而誇勍鱼域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1376296_comment'></div>夫著言纪事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1376296_comment'></div>在演致于全篇。<div id='poem_sentence_80_1376296_comment'></div>盖止交游之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1376296_comment'></div>僭将罪我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1376296_comment'></div>益知褒采之难。<div id='poem_sentence_86_1376296_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: -----title
大荔
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='873317c8c5ee4c9b8896ce00d3c54b8b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("873317c8c5ee4c9b8896ce00d3c54b8b");'><span id='873317c8c5ee4c9b8896ce00d3c54b8b_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=866&endYear=866')">866年</a>　本年秋，图去拜访王凝，并撰文。作品：《太原王公同州修堰记》<div id='poem_1376263' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376263' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376263?labeling=true' target='_blank'>太原王公同州修堰记</a><span class='authorDate'>（866年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14662, "唐末", "司空图", "poem_title_1376263")'>司空图</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376263_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376263'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376263'>洛自西北趣大河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376263_comment'></div>盖同源于积石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376263_comment'></div>伏而乃发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376263_comment'></div>离而复合耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376263_comment'></div>故其流皆浑而悍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376263_comment'></div>暴而难制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376263_comment'></div>然左辅土田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376263_comment'></div>赖之为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1376263", 1376263, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>膏壤</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376263_comment'></div>堰虽劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376263_comment'></div>不可废也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376263_comment'></div>而又振泥加厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376263_comment'></div>水势益抑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376263_comment'></div>去故治之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376263_comment'></div>治之勤日倍也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376263_comment'></div>大中末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376263_comment'></div>州南堰坏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376263_comment'></div>久不能复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376263_comment'></div>比岁旱蝗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376263_comment'></div>关畿尤困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376263_comment'></div>咸通五年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376263_comment'></div>太原王公自中书舍人出牧是邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376263_comment'></div>思所以利人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376263_comment'></div>无易于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376263_comment'></div>乃省公用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376263_comment'></div>节私费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376263_comment'></div>僦徒赋役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376263_comment'></div>躬亲率属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376263_comment'></div>得健吏于班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376263_comment'></div>授以成规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376263_comment'></div>亦既集事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376263_comment'></div>而中作雨甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376263_comment'></div>川壑会流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376263_comment'></div>雷风蹴南而鼓之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376263_comment'></div>益肆狂啮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376263_comment'></div>虽有力者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376263_comment'></div>坚百仞之阜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376263_comment'></div>亘为其防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376263_comment'></div>亦不能御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376263_comment'></div>势明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376263_comment'></div>必俟至诚克敷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376263_comment'></div>旁资感效耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376263_comment'></div>公晨往河壖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376263_comment'></div>跪陈牢醴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376263_comment'></div>既而阴云溃散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376263_comment'></div>功倍人悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376263_comment'></div>翌日堰乃成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376263_comment'></div>水折而东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376263_comment'></div>皆若导而徙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376263_comment'></div>令邑里交贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376263_comment'></div>合乐以迓之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376263_comment'></div>流闻京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1376263_comment'></div>中外以为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_51_1376263", 1376263, "Clauses/51/Comments/0")'>国庆</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1376263_comment'></div>时国家兵役屡兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1376263_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_53_1376263", 1376263, "Clauses/53/Comments/0")'>漕挽</span>已绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1376263_comment'></div>故自淮汴至于河潼之交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1376263_comment'></div>百敖皆刳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1376263_comment'></div>人无所仰视之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1376263_comment'></div>虽已鼎食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1376263_comment'></div>亦若衔馁而返。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1376263_comment'></div>农饥卒怠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1376263_comment'></div>何以振其威力哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1376263_comment'></div>关中不涸之辙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1376263_comment'></div>必本是堰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1376263_comment'></div>公果成之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1376263_comment'></div>以明大计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1376263_comment'></div>虽旋亦决败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1376263_comment'></div>而功绪足遗后人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1376263_comment'></div>七年秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1376263_comment'></div>愚自满获展贽见之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1376263_comment'></div>出次近坰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1376263_comment'></div>备得其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1376263_comment'></div>因著于篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1376263_comment'></div>以彰<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_72_1376263", 1376263, "Clauses/72/Comments/0")'>勤济</span>之志云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_72_1376263_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
宣城
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='28e53e2076f14dd1b25d7d0db745d0b0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("28e53e2076f14dd1b25d7d0db745d0b0");'><span id='28e53e2076f14dd1b25d7d0db745d0b0_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=877&endYear=878')">877-878年</a>，41-42岁</div><div id='28e53e2076f14dd1b25d7d0db745d0b0' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=877&endYear=877')">877年</a>　图随王凝入宣州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=878&endYear=878')">878年4—5月</a>　约于本年四五月，朝廷征图为殿中侍御史，图不忍离开恩师王凝，未及时赴任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=878&endYear=878')">878年8月7日</a>　图恩师王凝卒，图为其写行状。作品：《唐故宣州观察使检校礼部王公行状》<div id='poem_1376308' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376308' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376308?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故宣州观察使检校礼部王公行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（878年8月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14662, "唐末", "司空图", "poem_title_1376308")'>司空图</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376308_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376308'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376308'>曾祖翃，皇任御史大夫，赠户部尚书，谥忠惠公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376308_comment'></div>祖重，皇任河东县令，赠潞州都督。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376308_comment'></div>父众仲，皇任衡州刺史，赠司空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376308_comment'></div>公讳凝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376308_comment'></div>字成庶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376308_comment'></div>太原人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376308_comment'></div>礼法冠昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376308_comment'></div>著于雅族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376308_comment'></div>国朝忠惠公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376308_comment'></div>克振农烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376308_comment'></div>而河东衡州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376308_comment'></div>皆德优位下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376308_comment'></div>宜其集祉于当世也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376308_comment'></div>公幼孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376308_comment'></div>英发有神检。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376308_comment'></div>整襟受业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376308_comment'></div>瑞气郁然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376308_comment'></div>群辈莫敢轻狎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376308_comment'></div>相公郑公肃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376308_comment'></div>实公舅也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376308_comment'></div>一见<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1376308", 1376308, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>耸异</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376308_comment'></div>命子约为师友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376308_comment'></div>孝爱识度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376308_comment'></div>宜其大成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376308_comment'></div>年十五举孝廉上第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376308_comment'></div>其为文根六经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376308_comment'></div>必先劝试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376308_comment'></div>著都邑六冈铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376308_comment'></div>益振时誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376308_comment'></div>魏相国扶主贡籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376308_comment'></div>选中甲科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376308_comment'></div>崔公操首辟鹾府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376308_comment'></div>周相国墀镇东蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376308_comment'></div>裴公休廉问宣城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376308_comment'></div>操币者交于门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376308_comment'></div>视其所知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376308_comment'></div>知其立矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376308_comment'></div>崔公龟从入相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376308_comment'></div>拜鄠县尉校理集贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376308_comment'></div>孔公温业镇宣州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376308_comment'></div>辟为上介。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376308_comment'></div>韦公有翼初为御史丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376308_comment'></div>盛选僚属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376308_comment'></div>公首状拜监察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376308_comment'></div>会鄂州盐铁使赃状上闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376308_comment'></div>有力者持为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_45_1376308", 1376308, "Clauses/52/Comments/0")'>滞狱</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376308_comment'></div>公驰传即讯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376308_comment'></div>涉旬<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_47_1376308", 1376308, "Clauses/54/Comments/0")'>辨决</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376308_comment'></div>转殿中侍御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376308_comment'></div>崔魏公出抚淮甸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376308_comment'></div>奏为节度判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1376308_comment'></div>始以省秩命服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1376308_comment'></div>似助准的。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1376308_comment'></div>著之美谭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1376308_comment'></div>崔太保慎由浙西又拜徵左史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1376308_comment'></div>而大誇得人之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1376308_comment'></div>迁礼部员外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1376308_comment'></div>宣宗朝尝待制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1376308_comment'></div>独被顾问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1376308_comment'></div>正色谠言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1376308_comment'></div>不附权戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1376308_comment'></div>及内署进拟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1376308_comment'></div>竟为所挤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1376308_comment'></div>历兵部考功员外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1376308_comment'></div>前史称第一流必为第一官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1376308_comment'></div>唯公资望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1376308_comment'></div>人谓无愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1376308_comment'></div>转司封郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1376308_comment'></div>相国萧公寘判版籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1376308_comment'></div>请公分佐其务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1376308_comment'></div>俄拜长安令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1376308_comment'></div>政无私挠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1376308_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_72_1376308", 1376308, "Clauses/79/Comments/0")'>奸猾</span>革心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1376308_comment'></div>郑公处诲总宪纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1376308_comment'></div>公以考功郎中知杂事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1376308_comment'></div>不示<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_75_1376308", 1376308, "Clauses/82/Comments/0")'>峻厉</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1376308_comment'></div>僚吏自肃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1376308_comment'></div>相国夏侯公用为中书舍人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1376308_comment'></div>旋以同列或非清议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1376308_comment'></div>遂移疾乞免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1376308_comment'></div>拜同州防御使兼御史中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1376308_comment'></div>赐金紫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1376308_comment'></div>励精为治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1376308_comment'></div>表率列城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1376308_comment'></div>吏民守阙乞留遮道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1376308_comment'></div>宰相言状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1376308_comment'></div>上降玺书褒允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1376308_comment'></div>竟谢疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1376308_comment'></div>葺居华下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1376308_comment'></div>中外之议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1376308_comment'></div>谓公不司文柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1376308_comment'></div>为朝廷<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_91_1376308", 1376308, "Clauses/98/Comments/0")'>阙政</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1376308_comment'></div>竟拜礼部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1376308_comment'></div>韦澄迈在内廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1376308_comment'></div>悬入相之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1376308_comment'></div>其弟保殷干进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1376308_comment'></div>自谓殊等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1376308_comment'></div>不疑党附者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1376308_comment'></div>又方据权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1376308_comment'></div>亦多请托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1376308_comment'></div>攘臂傲视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1376308_comment'></div>人为寒心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1376308_comment'></div>公显言拒绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1376308_comment'></div>及榜出沸腾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1376308_comment'></div>以为近朝难事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1376308_comment'></div>噫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1376308_comment'></div>仁人之勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1376308_comment'></div>其可力夺哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1376308_comment'></div>久之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1376308_comment'></div>时宰竟用抗己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1376308_comment'></div>内不能平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1376308_comment'></div>遂至商于之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1376308_comment'></div>尚书御史大夫以塞群议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1376308_comment'></div>商病属邑颇滨于都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1376308_comment'></div>主吏骤更。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1376308_comment'></div>破产而不给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1376308_comment'></div>南鄙山阻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1376308_comment'></div>属役尤难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1376308_comment'></div>公俾相资赡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1376308_comment'></div>得以均济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1376308_comment'></div>又治赋羡银。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1376308_comment'></div>例皆推估以优俸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1376308_comment'></div>公命即赍月市驿驷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1376308_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_123_1376308", 1376308, "Clauses/130/Comments/0")'>横扰</span>既绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1376308_comment'></div>谣讼溢境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1376308_comment'></div>明年加检校常侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1376308_comment'></div>廉问湖外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1376308_comment'></div>理潭如商。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1376308_comment'></div>罔不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_128_1376308", 1376308, "Clauses/135/Comments/0")'>慰悦</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_317_1376308_comment'></div>必宏声价。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_318_1376308_comment'></div>未浼<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_319_1376308", 1376308, id='poem_sentence_321_1376308_comment'></div>方启<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_322_1376308", 1376308, "Clauses/329/Comments/0")'>钓川</span>之兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_322_1376308_comment'></div>俄缠罢市之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_323_1376308_comment'></div>悫实不彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_324_1376308_comment'></div>清尘遽远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_325_1376308_comment'></div>褒扬未尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_326_1376308_comment'></div>增一字而何惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_332_1376308_comment'></div>必光佥议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_333_1376308_comment'></div>谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_334_1376308_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=878&endYear=878')">878年</a>　图为王凝卒而请礼部赐谥号以旌表，撰文。作品：《上考功》<br /><a href="javascript: class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376295_comment'></div>非欲贩山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376295_comment'></div>知在木而无堪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376295_comment'></div>便当为社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376295_comment'></div>莫敢张皇丘壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376295_comment'></div>拟议巢由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376295_comment'></div>且自诏求贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376295_comment'></div>多因肆眚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376295_comment'></div>盖乘运泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376295_comment'></div>莫顾才难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376295_comment'></div>今上哲御临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376295_comment'></div>元勋振服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376295_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1376295", 1376295, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>英衮</span>赞<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1376295", 1376295, "Clauses/25/Comments/1")'>翘勤</span>之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376295_comment'></div>幽人荷<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1376295", 1376295, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>旌贲</span>之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376295_comment'></div>虽云例追。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376295_comment'></div>亦谓优礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376295_comment'></div>但巳伸拜阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376295_comment'></div>况毕悬车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376295_comment'></div>冀修知难之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376295_comment'></div>免冒<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1376295", 1376295, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>嚵荣</span>之诮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376295_comment'></div>昔江表则赋诗而褒孔令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376295_comment'></div>汉廷则出饯而宠疏翁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376295_comment'></div>特振孤芳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376295_comment'></div>实标胜事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376295_comment'></div>今也龙门回望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376295_comment'></div>鹤盖交驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376295_comment'></div>落日琴尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376295_comment'></div>前朝图画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376295_comment'></div>想家山之醉石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376295_comment'></div>认客处之渔舟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376295_comment'></div>白首归心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376295_comment'></div>黄花缘路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376295_comment'></div>来时不下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376295_comment'></div>漂零海上之鸥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376295_comment'></div>去兮自怜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376295_comment'></div>放旷人间之世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376295_comment'></div>斯乃仅能忘怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376295_comment'></div>庶可息机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1376295_comment'></div>敢慕高风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1376295_comment'></div>猥烦众作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1376295_comment'></div>诗家此会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1376295_comment'></div>谁邀清夜之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1376295_comment'></div>仙装不回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1376295_comment'></div>别有白云之集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1376295_comment'></div>徒攀逸唱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1376295_comment'></div>益愧<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_58_1376295", 1376295, "Clauses/58/Comments/0")'>馁才</span>。</div><div id='poem_sentence_58_1376295_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=905&endYear=905')">905年10月</a>　九月十日，卢渥卒，十月葬，图为其撰《唐故太子太师致仕卢公神道碑》<div id='poem_1376303' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376303' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376303?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故太子太师致仕卢公神道碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（905年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14662, "唐末", "司空图", "poem_title_1376303")'>司空图</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376303_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376303'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376303'>公讳渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376303_comment'></div>字子章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376303_comment'></div>范阳人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376303_comment'></div>卢氏出于齐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376303_comment'></div>齐之始祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376303_comment'></div>以姬周克享于仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376303_comment'></div>乃佐文武定天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376303_comment'></div>弛刑之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376303_comment'></div>其裔孙又能以大义<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1376303", 1376303, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>匡奉</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376303_comment'></div>且救诸侯之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376303_comment'></div>宜其百代昌盛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376303_comment'></div>及拓跋陷幽冀之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376303_comment'></div>士人之整饬官姻不失其旧者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376303_comment'></div>推于周党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376303_comment'></div>所为甲门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376303_comment'></div>高齐恩通公为黄门远公八世祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376303_comment'></div>曾祖某官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376303_comment'></div>祖某官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376303_comment'></div>皆以德义显本朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376303_comment'></div>先公讳某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376303_comment'></div>兼以儒术吏治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376303_comment'></div>历仕终某州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376303_comment'></div>娶清河夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376303_comment'></div>生公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376303_comment'></div>公植德秉仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376303_comment'></div>而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1376303", 1376303, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>识致</span>远大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376303_comment'></div>济之强学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376303_comment'></div>发为文章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376303_comment'></div>故未就乡学举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376303_comment'></div>则时辈后生皆以为杰出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376303_comment'></div>虽文场迂滞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376303_comment'></div>然时者亦历指<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_1376303", 1376303, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>要显</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376303_comment'></div>不敢徒以负地待之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376303_comment'></div>会府方重首荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376303_comment'></div>公为主试者所强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376303_comment'></div>举子未效其业于主师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376303_comment'></div>则踵门投贽者已数百辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376303_comment'></div>时宣宗锐意文治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376303_comment'></div>白衣稍出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376303_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1376303", 1376303, "Clauses/39/Comments/0")'>流类</span>亦往往上门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376303_comment'></div>故公中选甲科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376303_comment'></div>籍则待制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376303_comment'></div>名臣亦以得人为贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376303_comment'></div>皆为儒风隆替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376303_comment'></div>当系于公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376303_comment'></div>累辟诸侯府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376303_comment'></div>亦以公去就为轻重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376303_comment'></div>御史丞将选僚属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376303_comment'></div>递相告约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376303_comment'></div>才及升班之限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376303_comment'></div>台命已行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1376303_comment'></div>太夫人在洛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1376303_comment'></div>乞以散秩就养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1376303_comment'></div>拜国子博士分务殆十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1376303_comment'></div>公议所迫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1376303_comment'></div>迁侍御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1376303_comment'></div>专领东台之务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1376303_comment'></div>徵起居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1376303_comment'></div>转司封员外知杂事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1376303_comment'></div>正色谠言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1376303_comment'></div>举劾不挠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1376303_comment'></div>迁司勋郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1376303_comment'></div>时宰所忌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1376303_comment'></div>出倅宣武军以缓之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1376303_comment'></div>未更岁入为某曹郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1376303_comment'></div>迁拜万年令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1376303_comment'></div>大京兆每引见必优礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1376303_comment'></div>言则规禀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1376303_comment'></div>诸曹请事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1376303_comment'></div>若奉严师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1376303_comment'></div>其政可知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1376303_comment'></div>诰命极选所以内训百辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1376303_comment'></div>外训四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1376303_comment'></div>元和中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1376303_comment'></div>若韩李二文公裴晋公令狐相国元白李淮南联处内外之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1376303_comment'></div>任征伐约束。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1376303_comment'></div>佽助大朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1376303_comment'></div>其后取人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1376303_comment'></div>多以时望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1376303_comment'></div>望胜则人以地优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1376303_comment'></div>用轻则才以势轧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1376303_comment'></div>兼而不怍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1376303_comment'></div>乃属于公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1376303_comment'></div>拜某官知制诰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1376303_comment'></div>每涉委廉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1376303_comment'></div>则堂列耸眙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1376303_comment'></div>宰相详议大政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1376303_comment'></div>亦俟入直乃行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1376303_comment'></div>前后六年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1376303_comment'></div>编录盈笥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1376303_comment'></div>实一时之典则也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1376303_comment'></div>丁内忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1376303_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_92_1376303", 1376303, "Clauses/92/Comments/0")'>哀毁</span>逾礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1376303_comment'></div>士大夫莫不感伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1376303_comment'></div>免丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1376303_comment'></div>拜陕虢观察使兼御史中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1376303_comment'></div>前涖是邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1376303_comment'></div>或出禁侣恇畏内臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1376303_comment'></div>护军刘重美党类<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_98_1376303", 1376303, "Clauses/98/Comments/0")'>豪侈</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1376303_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_99_1376303", 1376303, "Clauses/99/Comments/0")'>傲视</span>廉使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1376303_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_100_1376303", 1376303, "Clauses/100/Comments/0")'>橐奸</span>黩货。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1376303_comment'></div>得以自专。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1376303_comment'></div>及公至镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1376303_comment'></div>待之有制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1376303_comment'></div>重美虽渐<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_104_1376303", 1376303, "Clauses/104/Comments/0")'>敛束</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1376303_comment'></div>故态未锄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1376303_comment'></div>公举其坏政之甚者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1376303_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_107_1376303", 1376303, "Clauses/107/Comments/0")'>面数</span>以挫其锋气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1376303_comment'></div>卒俛首受教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1376303_comment'></div>权不外夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1376303_comment'></div>教人自苏息矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1376303_comment'></div>遇江岭宿兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1376303_comment'></div>边戍乏食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1376303_comment'></div>滑州军奋臂标回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1376303_comment'></div>开折天侣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1376303_comment'></div>及骤至墙下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1376303_comment'></div>吏士缩慄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1376303_comment'></div>皆请闭关拒守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1376303_comment'></div>公曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1376303_comment'></div>彼冻馁所迫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1376303_comment'></div>未闻肆毒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1376303_comment'></div>吾因而抚之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1376303_comment'></div>冀其返善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1376303_comment'></div>若首唱其恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1376303_comment'></div>彼畏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_124_1376303", 1376303, "Clauses/124/Comments/0")'>彰闻</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1376303_comment'></div>则怀疑<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_125_1376303", 1376303, "Clauses/125/Comments/0")'>蜂溃</span>矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1376303_comment'></div>廷议力未能制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1376303_comment'></div>且当遏其所归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1376303_comment'></div>奈何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1376303_comment'></div>反开门具饩劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1376303_comment'></div>召主将亲谕之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1376303_comment'></div>果遽感悟而东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1376303_comment'></div>逮出境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1376303_comment'></div>人无罹其患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1376303_comment'></div>噫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1376303_comment'></div>古所谓仁勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1376303_comment'></div>难哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1376303_comment'></div>其他惠爱廉平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1376303_comment'></div>犹可徵诸故老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1376303_comment'></div>初公报政当陟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1376303_comment'></div>且悬文柄之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1376303_comment'></div>权倖所沮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1376303_comment'></div>事未克行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1376303_comment'></div>及此传闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1376303_comment'></div>中外推敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1376303_comment'></div>故宰职得伸其所志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1376303_comment'></div>冬十月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1376303_comment'></div>拜礼部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1376303_comment'></div>群辈之躁聚势门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1376303_comment'></div>欲以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_149_1376303", 1376303, "Clauses/149/Comments/0")'>浮论</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_149_1376303", 1376303, "Clauses/149/Comments/1")'>笼驾</span>主司者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1376303_comment'></div>迎自咎其牙角。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1376303_comment'></div>洎入贡署。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1376303_comment'></div>才引明经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1376303_comment'></div>则美称已哗于外议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1376303_comment'></div>遇大驾南幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1376303_comment'></div>乃中辍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1376303_comment'></div>人至今惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1376303_comment'></div>明年春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1376303_comment'></div>自都潜出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1376303_comment'></div>二月至中条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1376303_comment'></div>舍于幕吏司空图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1376303_comment'></div>被疾浃旬方至洛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1376303_comment'></div>由汉阴诣蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1376303_comment'></div>舟行迂滞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1376303_comment'></div>尚以后至授国子祭酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1376303_comment'></div>公论逾郁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1376303_comment'></div>拜御史丞兼左丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1376303_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_167_1376303", 1376303, "Clauses/167/Comments/0")'>柬拔</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_167_1376303", 1376303, "Clauses/167/Comments/1")'>端良</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1376303_comment'></div>风威益振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1376303_comment'></div>驾回未几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1376303_comment'></div>又徒步扈从于宝鸡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1376303_comment'></div>至褒中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1376303_comment'></div>歧蜀阻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1376303_comment'></div>兵食俱困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1376303_comment'></div>主相深念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1376303_comment'></div>计无所施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1376303_comment'></div>乃拜公户部尚书领兴元留事知节度使事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1376303_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_177_1376303", 1376303, "Clauses/177/Comments/0")'>焚剽</span>之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1376303_comment'></div>百姓逃窜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1376303_comment'></div>公躬自招抚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1376303_comment'></div>且徵赋食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1376303_comment'></div><span
