class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1376303_comment'></div>时议以为萧何大勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1376303_comment'></div>实非公不济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1376303_comment'></div>上每敛容优异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1376303_comment'></div>许以入辅者数矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1376303_comment'></div>公坚让乞退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1376303_comment'></div>至京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1376303_comment'></div>尚以检校司空太常卿畴庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1376303_comment'></div>迁尚书右仆射。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1376303_comment'></div>自古澄汰稍厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1376303_comment'></div>多碍于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1376303_comment'></div>苟訾失实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1376303_comment'></div>则受制群党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1376303_comment'></div>驱之仇敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1376303_comment'></div>反为国病矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1376303_comment'></div>公谓轨律在已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1376303_comment'></div>足以正人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1376303_comment'></div>未尝惑爱憎之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1376303_comment'></div>遽出升黜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1376303_comment'></div>而尤者自去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1376303_comment'></div>明恕以彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1376303_comment'></div>又古所谓得大臣之体者乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1376303_comment'></div>仁哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1376303_comment'></div>累授保傅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1376303_comment'></div>寻以检校司徒致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1376303_comment'></div>从坚请也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1376303_comment'></div>大驾<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_208_1376303", 1376303, "Clauses/208/Comments/0")'>移幸</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1376303_comment'></div>公自华至洛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1376303_comment'></div>天祐二年九月十日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1376303_comment'></div>寝疾薨于长寿佛宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1376303_comment'></div>享年八十六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1376303_comment'></div>嗣王辍朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1376303_comment'></div>赠某官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1376303_comment'></div>谥曰某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1376303_comment'></div>噫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1376303_comment'></div>古之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_217_1376303", 1376303, "Clauses/217/Comments/0")'>硕贤</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1376303_comment'></div>或享高位上寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1376303_comment'></div>盖尸其柄者时显至公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1376303_comment'></div>以警于昭幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1376303_comment'></div>俾为善者不悔耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1376303_comment'></div>公孝于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1376303_comment'></div>勤于国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1376303_comment'></div>宜于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1376303_comment'></div>既于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1376303_comment'></div>而报应又如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1376303_comment'></div>果使后之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_227_1376303", 1376303, "Clauses/227/Comments/0")'>追企</span>者唯恐不逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1376303_comment'></div>以邀福于神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1376303_comment'></div>然则善人之化于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1376303_comment'></div>虽没世而弥彰矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1376303_comment'></div>且家邦将盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_231_1376303_comment'></div>必有所繄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_232_1376303_comment'></div>盖感致之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1376303_comment'></div>当究其源耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1376303_comment'></div>初公既属文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1376303_comment'></div>太夫人知其友爱诸弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1376303_comment'></div>且命相<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_237_1376303", 1376303, "Clauses/237/Comments/0")'>敦诱</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1376303_comment'></div>故诸弟子亦能相师禀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1376303_comment'></div>就其所业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_239_1376303_comment'></div>及公中第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1376303_comment'></div>即又孜孜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_241_1376303", 1376303, "Clauses/241/Comments/0")'>指导</span>进取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_241_1376303_comment'></div>果岁继捷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_242_1376303_comment'></div>皆籍于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_243_1376303", 1376303, "Clauses/243/Comments/0")'>显地</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_243_1376303_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_244_1376303", 1376303, "Clauses/244/Comments/0")'>禄养</span>之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_244_1376303_comment'></div>孝敬之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_245_1376303_comment'></div>一时罕及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_246_1376303_comment'></div>推是而言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_247_1376303_comment'></div>则诗所谓施于兄弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_248_1376303_comment'></div>至于家邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_249_1376303_comment'></div>公宜与圣人之徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_250_1376303_comment'></div>亘百代而合契美哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_251_1376303_comment'></div>公介弟尚书公绍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_252_1376303_comment'></div>尤检剋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_253_1376303_comment'></div>亦能率其子弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_254_1376303_comment'></div>俾幼无违者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_255_1376303_comment'></div>仲弟治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_256_1376303_comment'></div>考功郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_257_1376303_comment'></div>季弟沈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_258_1376303_comment'></div>右补阙从事洛都留守府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_259_1376303_comment'></div>盖雅族积祐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_260_1376303_comment'></div>有以保持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_261_1376303_comment'></div>公以其年十月某日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_262_1376303_comment'></div>附葬于缑氏某乡某里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_263_1376303_comment'></div>礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_264_1376303_comment'></div>夫人姑臧君李氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_265_1376303_comment'></div>柔顺明淑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_266_1376303_comment'></div>叶公慈恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_267_1376303_comment'></div>内外孤婺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_268_1376303_comment'></div>赖之获济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_269_1376303_comment'></div>先公而终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_270_1376303_comment'></div>孤刑部侍郎膺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_271_1376303_comment'></div>实惟冢嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_272_1376303_comment'></div>敏材慎行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_273_1376303_comment'></div>而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_274_1376303", 1376303, "Clauses/274/Comments/0")'>嚣竞</span>不能入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_274_1376303_comment'></div>弟赓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_275_1376303_comment'></div>左补阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_276_1376303_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_277_1376303", 1376303, "Clauses/277/Comments/0")'>整整</span>唯谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_277_1376303_comment'></div>目为令人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_278_1376303_comment'></div>有以见绵祚无穷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_279_1376303_comment'></div>自昔负大名拥大望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_280_1376303_comment'></div>苟无其实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_281_1376303_comment'></div>必若负重而趋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_282_1376303_comment'></div>虽非有力者挤之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_283_1376303_comment'></div>亦当自蹶矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_284_1376303_comment'></div>宣懿之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_285_1376303_comment'></div>士类方竞其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_286_1376303_comment'></div>与公别著亲友之分者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_287_1376303_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_288_1376303", 1376303, "Clauses/288/Comments/0")'>崱崱</span>当世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_288_1376303_comment'></div>止有数贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_289_1376303_comment'></div>皆退可革天下之浇风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_290_1376303_comment'></div>进可效荷天下之大任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_291_1376303_comment'></div>殁则金石之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_292_1376303_comment'></div>缀史氏之笔端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_293_1376303_comment'></div>岂容易而品级哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_294_1376303_comment'></div>千载之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_295_1376303_comment'></div>必得其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_296_1376303_comment'></div>盖知始无愧耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_297_1376303_comment'></div>今年秋八月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_298_1376303_comment'></div>愚诏追洛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_299_1376303_comment'></div>拜公床下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_300_1376303_comment'></div>明日继谒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_301_1376303_comment'></div>蒙手授以诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_302_1376303_comment'></div>且有释氏多言宿分深之句。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_303_1376303_comment'></div>瞪视不言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_304_1376303_comment'></div>若属意于纪述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_305_1376303_comment'></div>默至感悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_306_1376303_comment'></div>誓竭菲才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_307_1376303_comment'></div>况业履谟庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_308_1376303_comment'></div>三纪备熟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_309_1376303_comment'></div>虽有文酋之工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_310_1376303_comment'></div>亦莫能详悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_311_1376303_comment'></div>然则刊尔信实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_312_1376303_comment'></div>门人焉得为让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_313_1376303_comment'></div>铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_314_1376303_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_315_1376303'>姜佐宗姬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_315_1376303_comment'></div>仁移于谊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_316_1376303_comment'></div>驰及厥裔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_317_1376303_comment'></div>亦恢四履。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_318_1376303_comment'></div>纫绝扶微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_319_1376303_comment'></div>益延世祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_320_1376303_comment'></div>战国横溃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_321_1376303_comment'></div>独整士风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_322_1376303_comment'></div>汉氏之东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_323_1376303_comment'></div>植显大宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_324_1376303_comment'></div>黄门魁伟。<div id='poem_sentence_327_1376303_comment'></div>教义足维。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_328_1376303_comment'></div>出入允宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_329_1376303_comment'></div>万方廷萃。<div id='poem_sentence_332_1376303_comment'></div>秉文慎择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_333_1376303_comment'></div>列曹骤历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_334_1376303_comment'></div>乃训百辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_335_1376303_comment'></div>国事洞疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_336_1376303_comment'></div>王旅阻饥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_337_1376303_comment'></div>惟公是咨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_338_1376303_comment'></div>冠裳奕奕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_339_1376303_comment'></div>礼义是则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_340_1376303_comment'></div>公庸乃陟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_341_1376303_comment'></div>或道之亨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_342_1376303_comment'></div>孰喜孰戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_343_1376303_comment'></div>华崇之趾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_344_1376303_comment'></div>吾老如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_345_1376303_comment'></div>克跻寿祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_346_1376303_comment'></div>皆极报德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_347_1376303_comment'></div>照彼日星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_348_1376303_comment'></div>摩地载扃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_349_1376303_comment'></div>镵石张铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_350_1376303_comment'></div>济我淑贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_351_1376303_comment'></div>勖尔后生。</div><div 华阴

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=889&endYear=889')">889年10月</a>　秋，十月，图为王重荣之母作墓志。作品：《蒲帅燕国太夫人石氏墓志》<div id='poem_1376307' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376307' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_1376307'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376307'>尝览淑德之传多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376307_comment'></div>其有存所以保千钟之养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376307_comment'></div>殁所以固九族之安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376307_comment'></div>始著宜家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376307_comment'></div>终由训子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376307_comment'></div>遂致忠资报国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376307_comment'></div>叶宗社以贻休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376307_comment'></div>忧不贻亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376307_comment'></div>指山河而献寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376307_comment'></div>永惟作范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376307_comment'></div>必在择邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376307_comment'></div>今见之于太傅相公王公矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376307_comment'></div>夫人姓石氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376307_comment'></div>其先乐陵人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376307_comment'></div>积德浚源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376307_comment'></div>疏封命氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376307_comment'></div>勋华相焕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376307_comment'></div>名教所宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376307_comment'></div>碏著义方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376307_comment'></div>腾褒鲁史。<div id='poem_sentence_40_1376307_comment'></div>敌自穷于术内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376307_comment'></div>雄藩踠足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376307_comment'></div>位实冠于军中。<div id='poem_sentence_240_1376307_comment'></div>信惟兰而与菊。</div><div id='poem_sentence_241_1376307_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=889&endYear=889')">889年</a>　图在华阴得阅柳宗元全集，撰文。作品：《题柳柳州集后》<div id='poem_1376256' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376256' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376256?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题柳柳州集后序</a><span class='authorDate'>（889年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14662, "唐末", "司空图", "poem_title_1376256")'>司空图</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376256_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376256'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376256'>金之精粗。考其声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376256_comment'></div>皆可辨也。岂清于磬而浑于钟哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376256_comment'></div>然则作者为文为诗。才格亦可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376256_comment'></div>岂当善于彼而不善于此耶。愚观文人之为诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376256_comment'></div>诗人之为文。始皆系其所尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376256_comment'></div>既专则搜研愈至。故能衒其工于不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376256_comment'></div>亦犹力巨而斗者。所持之器各异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376256_comment'></div>而皆能<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1376256", 1376256, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>济胜</span>。以为勍敌也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376256_comment'></div>愚尝览韩吏部歌诗累百首。其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1376256", 1376256, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>驱驾</span>气势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376256_comment'></div>若掀雷抉电。奔腾于天地之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376256_comment'></div>物状奇变。不得不鼓舞而徇其呼吸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376256_comment'></div>其次皇甫祠部文集。所作亦为遒逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376256_comment'></div>非无意于深密。盖或未遑耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376256_comment'></div>今于华下方得柳诗。味其深搜之致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376256_comment'></div>亦深远矣。俾其穷而克寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376256_comment'></div>抗精极思。则固非琐琐者轻可拟议其优劣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376256_comment'></div>又尝睹杜子美祭太尉房公文李太白佛寺碑赞。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1376256", 1376256, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>宏拔</span>清厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376256_comment'></div>乃其歌诗也。张曲江五言沈郁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376256_comment'></div>亦其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1376256", 1376256, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>文笔</span>也。岂相伤哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376256_comment'></div>噫。彼之学者褊浅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376256_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1376256", 1376256, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>片词只句</span>。不能自辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376256_comment'></div>已侧目相诋訾矣。痛哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376256_comment'></div>因题柳集之末。庶俾后之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1376256", 1376256, "Clauses/45/Comments/0")'>诠评</span>者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376256_comment'></div>罔惑偏说。以盖其全工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376256_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1376256_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十八 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（891年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_11772_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_11772'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_11772'>此身衰病转堪嗟，长忍春寒独惜花。<div id='poem_sentence_0_11772_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_11772'>更恨新诗无纸写，蜀笺堆积是谁家。<div id='poem_sentence_1_11772_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_11772'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_11772_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_11773' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_11773' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/11773?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_11773'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_11773'>昨日黄昏始看回，梦中相约又衔杯。<div id='poem_sentence_0_11773_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_11773'>起来闻道风飘却，犹拟教人扫取来。<div id='poem_sentence_1_11773_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_11773'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_11773_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=891&endYear=891')">891年</a>　图寓居华阴，有诗。作品：《华岳庙裴晋公题名》<div id='poem_12064' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_12064' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/12064?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题裴晋公华岳庙题名</a><span class='authorDate'>（891年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14662, "唐末", "司空图", "poem_title_12064")'>司空图</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_12064_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_12064'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_12064'>岳前<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_12064", 12064, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>大队</span>赴淮西，从此中原息鼓<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作战）</span>鼙。<div id='poem_sentence_0_12064_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_12064'>石阙莫教苔藓上，分明认取晋公题。<div id='poem_sentence_1_12064_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_12064'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_12064_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=891&endYear=891')">891年</a>　图寓居华阴，有文。作品：《说鱼》<div id='poem_1376285' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376285' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376285?labeling=true' target='_blank'>说鱼</a><span class='authorDate'>（891年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14662, "唐末", "司空图", "poem_title_1376285")'>司空图</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376285_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376285'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376285'>蒲之东七十里。山秀而瘠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376285_comment'></div>故其水<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1376285", 1376285, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>迅激</span>。不能蓄<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1376285", 1376285, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>鬐介</span>之族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376285_comment'></div>著于方志焉。王城谷司空氏曰祯贻溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376285_comment'></div>其岩瀑尤为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1376285", 1376285, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>峭束</span>。愚尝派著于庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376285_comment'></div>欲资涵泳之玩。或致于他所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376285_comment'></div>亦不更夕辄暴去。前年捧诏西上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376285_comment'></div>复移疾华下。则邻之佛者遽至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376285_comment'></div>言石窦泉隙。鱼皆<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1376285", 1376285, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>充牣</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376285_comment'></div>愚熟念竟不能究其说。而佛者谓吾久于是溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376285_comment'></div>虽才啬而命弛。然抚其爱育之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376285_comment'></div>足以达其物类。盖斯鱼之产。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376285_comment'></div>是欲信吾心于方将耳。而愚尚以为愧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376285_comment'></div>且以为羁。涉岁而后鱼集于故山泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376285_comment'></div>彼能达吾之心。宅幽而远害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376285_comment'></div>是有物致之。且惑愚之妄进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376285_comment'></div>姑欲全吾道而退保安耳。敢不自警也哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376285_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1376285_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=892&endYear=892')">892年</a>　朝廷征图为谏议大夫，图称病不赴。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=892&endYear=892')">892年5月</a>　图奉敕为河中节度使王重盈撰《太尉琅玡王公生祠碑》<div id='poem_1376304' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376304' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376304?labeling=true' target='_blank'>太尉琅琊王公河中生祠碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（892年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14662, "唐末", "司空图", "poem_title_1376304")'>司空图</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376304_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376304'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376304'>臣伏念天人之庆。静则统和于天化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376304_comment'></div>动则保定于中兴。莫不肇拥元符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376304_comment'></div>已济昭登之德。旁徵幽契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376304_comment'></div>亦伸叶佐之能。内著弥纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376304_comment'></div>外宣风绩。克延休命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376304_comment'></div>共赞昌期。虽复地辅登皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376304_comment'></div>星枢延圣。八极柱断鳌之表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376304_comment'></div>百灵趋驾象之尘。信谓元方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376304_comment'></div>犹勤致乂。至若锡戈祚土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376304_comment'></div>赐履专征。止图九合之威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376304_comment'></div>亦赖五臣之佐。况顷者运属<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1376304", 1376304, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>履危</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376304_comment'></div>时当<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1376304", 1376304, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>戡难</span>。宇县尚摇于坱轨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376304_comment'></div>蜫蚊方骇于沸腾。欲拯横流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376304_comment'></div>是资杰出。汉庭剑履。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376304_comment'></div>名臣之礼秩皆优。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1376304", 1376304, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>烟阁</span>丹青。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376304_comment'></div>上将之风棱如在。我国家之御历也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376304_comment'></div>厚恢周德。宽富殷人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376304_comment'></div>荡千古而独驾雄图。掩八纮而同开寿域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376304_comment'></div>宏材构厦。常扶不拔之基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376304_comment'></div>犷俗倾风。尽仰升平之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376304_comment'></div>皇帝明融睿作。刚体乾行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376304_comment'></div>深研不测之机。广被无私之照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376304_comment'></div>常经多难。时亦濯征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376304_comment'></div>扫氛沴于灵旗。碎瓶罂于天斧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376304_comment'></div>文思<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1376304", 1376304, "Clauses/48/Comments/0")'>纬俗</span>。廓贞观之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1376304", 1376304, "Clauses/49/Comments/0")'>英图</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376304_comment'></div>神武定基。符开元之大业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376304_comment'></div>克谐注意。本在知臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376304_comment'></div>叶风力以陈谟。驾昆彭而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1376304", 1376304, "Clauses/55/Comments/0")'>骋绩</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376304_comment'></div>克绥中外。保奉宗祧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376304_comment'></div>大顺二年月日。首议陟明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376304_comment'></div>累宣恩诏。以命河中节度使王重盈加检校太傅兼中书令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376304_comment'></div>河汾蓄宝。阀阅资祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376304_comment'></div>代济贤豪。业传诗礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376304_comment'></div>自标<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1376304", 1376304, "Clauses/66/Comments/0")'>奇玮</span>。难藏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1376304", 1376304, "Clauses/67/Comments/0")'>豹蔚</span>之姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376304_comment'></div>本俟遭逢。果振螭蟠之举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376304_comment'></div>式膺妙简。允著宏规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376304_comment'></div>不有褒崇。孰明奖劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376304_comment'></div>且自古<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_37_1376304", 1376304, "Clauses/74/Comments/0")'>英达</span>致用。风范相殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376304_comment'></div>政则以理为先。化则以人为本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376304_comment'></div>虽或议参草昧。名列循良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376304_comment'></div>集东观之群儒。皆令赞像。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376304_comment'></div>推南山之汗简。尽使书勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376304_comment'></div>尚有间然。孰当全美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376304_comment'></div>道之必合。圣亦罕言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376304_comment'></div>大易所谓穷神。不言而速。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376304_comment'></div>哲人所以垂训。不令而从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376304_comment'></div>盖率以身先。用如响应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376304_comment'></div>公幼推至性。动必有方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376304_comment'></div>色养不违。友于兼备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376304_comment'></div>在闺庭而惟谨。处乡里而无尤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376304_comment'></div>卫公靖幼实师儒。宁妨勇烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1376304_comment'></div>英公绩贵能事长。果保宗良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1376304_comment'></div>是乃化己行于人子也。且移孝资忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1376304_comment'></div>自家移国。信风行而草偃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1376304_comment'></div>若传命于置邮。故乱离以前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1376304_comment'></div>委寄即重。效彰理剧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1376304_comment'></div>诚著让夷。课实最于西河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1376304_comment'></div>荣遂临于分陕。车未及境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1376304_comment'></div>寇已陷城。僵仆如邱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1376304_comment'></div>烟埃翳日。公乃唱大顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1376304_comment'></div>振义声。招葺逋逃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1376304_comment'></div>抚循疮痏。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_61_1376304", 1376304, "Clauses/123/Comments/0")'>诛榛薙梗</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1376304_comment'></div>渐辟乐郊。扑魅驱狸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1376304_comment'></div>潜消沴气。檄驰东夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1376304_comment'></div>馈赈西师。四海<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_64_1376304", 1376304, "Clauses/129/Comments/0")'>摇心</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1376304_comment'></div>尽摄鲸吞之势。重关失险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1376304_comment'></div>独当豕突之冲。壮我金汤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1376304_comment'></div>剖其牙角。实挫滔天之暴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1376304_comment'></div>非徒捍境之勤。大寇既逃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1376304_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_69_1376304", 1376304, "Clauses/138/Comments/0")'>邻封</span>共庆。遽求罢任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1376304_comment'></div>本切归宁。坚避<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_70_1376304", 1376304, "Clauses/141/Comments/0")'>成功</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1376304_comment'></div>益彰<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_71_1376304", 1376304, "Clauses/142/Comments/0")'>杰操</span>。是乃化己行于人臣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1376304_comment'></div>且恤刑育物。往哲至论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1376304_comment'></div>于兵法之中。亦叶道家之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1376304_comment'></div>虽战同<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_74_1376304", 1376304, "Clauses/148/Comments/0")'>九地</span>。或于危地争先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1376304_comment'></div>术用八方。乃以生门为上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1376304_comment'></div>勿轻士类。方保众心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1376304_comment'></div>盛衰之由。宽猛可验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1376304_comment'></div>雄名震敌。忌唯在于杀降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1376304_comment'></div>隆德传家。庆本延于慎狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1376304_comment'></div>公明为照。意在胜残。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1376304_comment'></div>深防巧诋之文。每用惟疑之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1376304_comment'></div>或有狂妄。自挂网罗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1376304_comment'></div>罪皆止于一身。恩必加于百口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1376304_comment'></div>神明<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_84_1376304", 1376304, "Clauses/168/Comments/0")'>洞感</span>。福佑宜钟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1376304_comment'></div>是乃化巳行于宰守也。夫<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_85_1376304", 1376304, "Clauses/171/Comments/0")'>约己</span>裕人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1376304_comment'></div>招怀必信。推诚体国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1376304_comment'></div>嫌衅自平。公实宽宏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1376304_comment'></div>且无猜沮。每示坦夷之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1376304_comment'></div>不行谗佞之言。延纳羁孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1376304_comment'></div>优容僚吏。位虽益重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1376304_comment'></div>谦则惟光。泛爱皆周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1376304_comment'></div>亲仁每见。宾贤备礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1376304_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_93_1376304", 1376304, "Clauses/186/Comments/0")'>耆英</span>尽缀于词林。将略求材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1376304_comment'></div>剑戟自森于武库。况路当冲要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1376304_comment'></div>时犒师徒。使车旁午于军中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1376304_comment'></div>将迎益至。羽檄交驰于境上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1376304_comment'></div>谈笑忘疲。志切<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_97_1376304", 1376304, "Clauses/195/Comments/0")'>匡扶</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1376304_comment'></div>义惟尊戴。每承诏命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1376304_comment'></div>若觐天颜。亦常因拜飞章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1376304_comment'></div>大集戎旅。誓坚金石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1376304_comment'></div>同报宠光。保九重高枕之无忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1376304_comment'></div>绝五夜甘泉之有警。内则颁宣朝旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1376304_comment'></div>外则镇抚人心。竟用<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_103_1376304", 1376304, "Clauses/207/Comments/0")'>绥和</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1376304_comment'></div>到今繄赖。是乃化巳行于藩阃也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1376304_comment'></div>且将图丰逸。必正本源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1376304_comment'></div>侈与骄期。莫能胜弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1376304_comment'></div>俭唯德固。乃不移风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1376304_comment'></div>苟曰聚人。必先济物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1376304_comment'></div>公幼负四方之志。家无一掷之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1376304_comment'></div>意气所倾。英豪共感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1376304_comment'></div>今则欲均公用。不树私恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1376304_comment'></div>动有常规。赏无滥费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1376304_comment'></div>上勤<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_113_1376304", 1376304, "Clauses/226/Comments/0")'>时贡</span>。下赡军须。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1376304_comment'></div>月未及于授衣。士已忻于挟纩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1376304_comment'></div>农商竞劝。役不夺时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1376304_comment'></div>关市薄征。肆无滞货。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1376304_comment'></div>利每推于近盬。惠岂计于伤威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1376304_comment'></div>靡尚虚名。多仍旧制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1376304_comment'></div>虽风亭月观。不增游玩之华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1376304_comment'></div>而城雉军营。足壮藩方之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1376304_comment'></div>均能劝勇。俭足<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_121_1376304", 1376304, "Clauses/243/Comments/0")'>养廉</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1376304_comment'></div>诫满持全。居丰处约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1376304_comment'></div>是乃化已行于闾里也。率是五者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1376304_comment'></div>施于一方。薰为和气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1376304_comment'></div>屡致嘉祥。故得疵疠不生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1376304_comment'></div>丰登相继。自窜渡河之兽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1376304_comment'></div>如驱避境之蝗。礼让俱兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1376304_comment'></div>人有耻格。征徭渐省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1376304_comment'></div>俗赖欢康。货殖殷繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1376304_comment'></div>井闾填咽。街无促步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1376304_comment'></div>巷有安歌。壮千叶之威棱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1376304_comment'></div>冠三河之富盛。关防旦启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1376304_comment'></div>谁候鸣鸡。徒侣宵行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1376304_comment'></div>罕闻吠犬。此盖罔存小察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1376304_comment'></div>唯总大纲。用宏宽简之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1376304_comment'></div>克赞雍熙之运。景福元年正月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1376304_comment'></div>上自将佐。下逮缁黄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1376304_comment'></div>五郡联属。四封耆艾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1376304_comment'></div>共忻宏庇。请建生祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1376304_comment'></div>牢让累陈。至诚难沮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1376304_comment'></div>五月日。都押衙录事参军又诣让军使特进思猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1376304_comment'></div>请奏别立碑纪。上亦俯从人愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1376304_comment'></div>有命微臣。伏以祀典阙文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1376304_comment'></div>朝恩特允。虽或徵于近史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1376304_comment'></div>亦宜本于众情。丞相仁杰之抚<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_145_1376304", 1376304, "Clauses/291/Comments/0")'>疲羸</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1376304_comment'></div>仆射元振之安夷夏。皆留<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_146_1376304", 1376304, "Clauses/293/Comments/0")'>盛躅</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1376304_comment'></div>孰继美谈。岂不若峻峙在前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1376304_comment'></div>人皆仰望。洪流非远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1376304_comment'></div>日可窥临。所以别创祠堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1376304_comment'></div>严陈像设者。盖皆蒙美利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1376304_comment'></div>并荷丰功。愿申报德之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1376304_comment'></div>别置表虔之所。且公抗衡右族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1376304_comment'></div>著籍本州。显沂水之华宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1376304_comment'></div>焕晋阳之贵冑。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_154_1376304", 1376304, "Clauses/309/Comments/0")'>盘联</span>日下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1376304_comment'></div>辉映关东。前修则家牒流芳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1376304_comment'></div>后嗣则卿材森列。公先君勋华早振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1376304_comment'></div>政绩频彰。巳结义于乡闾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1376304_comment'></div>仍种恩于部伍。永言积庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1376304_comment'></div>实异他门。况元昆顷镇河潼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1376304_comment'></div>远推<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_160_1376304", 1376304, "Clauses/320/Comments/0")'>表则</span>。仲弟镇临此地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1376304_comment'></div>惠爱斯人。季弟植性谦冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1376304_comment'></div>宣劳宿卫。次子今陕州相国能传善教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1376304_comment'></div>大济仁声。长子瓘故莅平阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1376304_comment'></div>季子瑶今为慈牧。并遵诰诫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1376304_comment'></div>皆禀廉明。诸子等庭列<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_165_1376304", 1376304, "Clauses/331/Comments/0")'>钟彝</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1376304_comment'></div>笥传组绶。靡忘承家之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1376304_comment'></div>方滋视履之祥。而公又领蒲之初也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1376304_comment'></div>深自窜伏。过于推奉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1376304_comment'></div>越人熏穴。盖虐求贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1376304_comment'></div>晋国乞盟。始闻定难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1376304_comment'></div>既抗言而誓众。方<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_171_1376304", 1376304, "Clauses/343/Comments/0")'>揽涕</span>以登车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1376304_comment'></div>里巷相欢。风云动色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1376304_comment'></div>宸衷夙注。宠诏遽临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1376304_comment'></div>致阖境之允洽。固本朝之是卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1376304_comment'></div>况家丰光烈。治陟殊尤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1376304_comment'></div>流寓安得不归。士庶安得不感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1376304_comment'></div>且自汉仪重整。周室甫宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1376304_comment'></div>三畿则横被隩区。九鼎则深盘王气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1376304_comment'></div>山河益壮。日月犹新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1376304_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_180_1376304", 1376304, "Clauses/360/Comments/0")'>心膂</span>连营。蓄雷霆于北落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1376304_comment'></div>股肱重镇。寄柱石于东门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1376304_comment'></div>允副分忧。合膺异渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1376304_comment'></div>宜其恢宏栋宇。瞻奉威容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1376304_comment'></div>上显圣慈。下谐人欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1376304_comment'></div>极当时之盛美。标抗古之殊荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1376304_comment'></div>美矣哉。臣迹本寓居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1376304_comment'></div>心非昧利。久怀<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_187_1376304", 1376304, "Clauses/375/Comments/0")'>赞激</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1376304_comment'></div>窃听讴谣。奉<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_188_1376304", 1376304, "Clauses/377/Comments/0")'>眷奖</span>于丝纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1376304_comment'></div>素惭鸿笔。图嘉庸于简册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1376304_comment'></div>先琢贞珉。方备编修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1376304_comment'></div>敢辞纪述。铭云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1376304_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_192_1376304", 1376304, "Clauses/384/Comments/0")'>贞符</span>奉我。诞命维唐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1376304_comment'></div>跨轹三古。牢笼万方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1376304_comment'></div>云蒸日煦。赆辇琛航。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1376304_comment'></div>基仁德厚。祚德逾昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1376304_comment'></div>数有屯夷。时婴否隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1376304_comment'></div>海岳摇荡。人祇愤激。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1376304_comment'></div>轩傒垂衣。舜勤舞戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1376304_comment'></div>皆安宠利。宜恤社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1376304_comment'></div>殷忧将变。兴运有开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1376304_comment'></div>涵濡动植。挥斥云雷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1376304_comment'></div>地岌重正。天旋更恢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1376304_comment'></div>畴庸乃眷。共致康哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1376304_comment'></div>宝鼎传铭。雄图作固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1376304_comment'></div>仪形九牧。光昭百度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1376304_comment'></div>威济家声。功宁国步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1376304_comment'></div>蒲人熙熙。是祷是祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1376304_comment'></div>孰歌且舞。童顶庞眉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1376304_comment'></div>何以祝之。祝公之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1376304_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_210_1376304", 1376304, "Clauses/420/Comments/0")'>险夷</span>不渝。保是宠禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1376304_comment'></div>何以祝之。祝公之寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1376304_comment'></div>左山右河。惟公克守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1376304_comment'></div>何以祝之。祝公宴喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1376304_comment'></div>公乐之人。如酒斯旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1376304_comment'></div>何以祝之。祝公之安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1376304_comment'></div>公安可久。附众惟宽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1376304_comment'></div>公之报国。人亦报公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1376304_comment'></div>提婴抚稚。必敬必忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1376304_comment'></div>人之报公。神亦报之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1376304_comment'></div>拂灾御暴。不流不移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1376304_comment'></div>通衢共仰。华搆崇之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1376304_comment'></div>峨冠<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_222_1376304", 1376304, "Clauses/444/Comments/0")'>杰表</span>。煦物温容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1376304_comment'></div>蔚然喜气。靡若和风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1376304_comment'></div>树之可爱。蒲之所赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1376304_comment'></div>帝慈允属。天鉴不昧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1376304_comment'></div>条峰颜颜。城在碑在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1376304_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_227_1376304_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=892&endYear=892')">892年</a>　图有文。作品：《注〈悯征赋〉述 》《注〈悯征赋〉后述 》<div id='poem_1376298' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376298' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376298?labeling=true' target='_blank'>注悯征赋后述</a><span class='authorDate'>（892年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14662, "唐末", "司空图", "poem_title_1376298")'>司空图</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376298_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376298'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376298'>武宣之间籍显地者。虽无如梁韩数公以雅实自任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376298_comment'></div>而能振拔后进。然士大夫宴游之倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376298_comment'></div>犹或时道文学以佽助执事者。而卢君尚以搀摈致愤于累千百言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376298_comment'></div>亦犹虎之饵毒。蛟之饮镞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376298_comment'></div>其作也。虽震邱林鼓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1376298", 1376298, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>溟涨</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376298_comment'></div>不能决其咆怒之气。且<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1376298", 1376298, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>科爵</span>之设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376298_comment'></div>是多得于彼而少丧于此。侈其虚而歉其实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376298_comment'></div>彼或充然自喜。而又以拱默相持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376298_comment'></div>曾不知日月没于晷刻之间。蝇翔而萤腐耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376298_comment'></div>然则著明幸于弃默。而能以悯征争勍于千载之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376298_comment'></div>吾知彼之作者。有呕血不能逮之者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376298_comment'></div>其所得何如于彼哉。且上至圣哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376298_comment'></div>下至<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1376298", 1376298, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>豪特</span>之士。得于文学者多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376298_comment'></div>岂以一灵运之狂。而可<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1376298", 1376298, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>沮辱</span>天下之奇伟哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376298_comment'></div>况面墙而悖谬者。何翅于此耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376298_comment'></div>愚前述虽巳恣道其遒壮悽艳矣。而终不能掩其方外之致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376298_comment'></div>以是掷笔狂叫。寄之他生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376298_comment'></div>又尝著濯缨引。以雪词人之愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376298_comment'></div>其旨亦属于卢君。且凡禀精爽之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376298_comment'></div>是或有智谋超出群辈。一旦愤抑肆其笔舌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376298_comment'></div>亦犹武人逞怒于锋刃也。俾其无所控告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376298_comment'></div>驱于雠敌。必贻国家之患矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376298_comment'></div>然则据权而蔽善者。得不常以此危虑哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376298_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1376298_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=893&endYear=893')">893年</a>　朝廷征拜图为户部侍郎，图赴阙，数日即辞归。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=893&endYear=893')">893年</a>　四明人孙合寄书与图，责图有退保之意，图撰文表其“不愿妄进”之意。作品：《答孙合书》<div id='poem_1376255' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376255' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376255?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答孙邰书</a><span class='authorDate'>（893年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14662, "唐末", "司空图", "poem_title_1376255")'>司空图</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376255_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376255'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376255'>孙君足下。所贶累幅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376255_comment'></div>皆厚责于我。是足下勤于吾道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376255_comment'></div>必欲起而振之也。何以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1376255", 1376255, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>克当</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376255_comment'></div>虽然。始于退者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376255_comment'></div>皆曰吾之必诚也。今愚独以为不诚<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1376255", 1376255, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>自讼</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376255_comment'></div>亦诚在其中矣。幸足下详其旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376255_comment'></div>古之山林者。必能简于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1376255", 1376255, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>情累</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376255_comment'></div>而后可久。今吾少也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376255_comment'></div>忿然不能自胜于胸中。及不诚而退者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376255_comment'></div>然亦穷而不摇。寻而不进者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376255_comment'></div>盖审已熟虽进亦不足于救时耳。彼一饭之施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376255_comment'></div>或请济于其邻。虽童子不可以空器绐之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376255_comment'></div>矧当<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1376255", 1376255, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>艰否</span>之运。吾君吾相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376255_comment'></div>方以爵秩来天下之贤达。将与之共拯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376255_comment'></div>其可沽虚而自集耶。且自古贤达用舍之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376255_comment'></div>当俟至公物情。而后天意可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376255_comment'></div>虽宰执大臣之推心。亦不能察天下拒我之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376255_comment'></div>况足下一布衣。其可独私于我哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376255_comment'></div>书曰。龟从蓍从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376255_comment'></div>则人亦不违天矣。足下所示。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376255_comment'></div>勤勤于此。而取舍之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376255_comment'></div>果致失坠是非有物亦欲沮之耶。始吾自视固<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1376255", 1376255, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>缺薄</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376255_comment'></div>今又益疑其不可妄进。且持危之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376255_comment'></div>制变之机。非鲰懦之所克辨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376255_comment'></div>愚虽不佞。亦为士夫独任其耻者久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376255_comment'></div>其可老而冒之耶。韩吏部激李桂州之不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376255_comment'></div>责阳道州无勇。虽致二贤适自困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376255_comment'></div>亦何救于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1376255", 1376255, "Clauses/54/Comments/0")'>大患</span>哉。其所为者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376255_comment'></div>或奋而不顾。匹夫匹妇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376255_comment'></div>亦可为之。孟子所谓非不能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376255_comment'></div>足下粹于通义耳。其间亦未尽于仆者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376255_comment'></div>勿多谭。再拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376255_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1376255_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=894&endYear=894')">894年</a>　本年六月后，图奉敕为华州节度使韩建撰《华帅许国公德政碑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈道贵《司空图生平与作品系年三题》（《文学遗产》2006年第2期）认为：《华帅许国公德政碑》当作于乾宁四年。）</span><div id='poem_1376306' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376306' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376306?labeling=true' target='_blank'>华帅许国公德政碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（894年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14662, "唐末", "司空图", "poem_title_1376306")'>司空图</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376306_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376306'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376306'>臣尝跪读贞观政要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376306_comment'></div>伏睹太宗文皇帝即位之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376306_comment'></div>每以为将致治平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376306_comment'></div>必先仁义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376306_comment'></div>在德贤而作乂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376306_comment'></div>乃锡祚而永延。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376306_comment'></div>古治足徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376306_comment'></div>格言可鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376306_comment'></div>岂不以化训则易服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376306_comment'></div>威肃则难齐者哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376306_comment'></div>然政教初张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376306_comment'></div>德刑具举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376306_comment'></div>文衰则削。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376306_comment'></div>将弊也其风必佻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376306_comment'></div>武渎则危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376306_comment'></div>将乱也其政必暴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376306_comment'></div>始于厚俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376306_comment'></div>方克<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1376306", 1376306, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>济和</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376306_comment'></div>视今足以知昔矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376306_comment'></div>圣唐照临万方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376306_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1376306", 1376306, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>韬轶</span>三代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376306_comment'></div>固资天力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376306_comment'></div>实廓帝图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376306_comment'></div>神灵蓄不测之威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376306_comment'></div>正朔被无垠之族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376306_comment'></div>皇帝中兴昌运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376306_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1376306", 1376306, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>丕显</span>耿光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376306_comment'></div>洞德泽于六幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376306_comment'></div>云蒸其润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376306_comment'></div>仰徽明于八表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376306_comment'></div>日焕其文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376306_comment'></div>内辅外藩而允谐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376306_comment'></div>上祇下肃而乃劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376306_comment'></div>太平之祉可固矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376306_comment'></div>乾宁元年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376306_comment'></div>上御便殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376306_comment'></div>遂出镇国监军使董重彦所奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376306_comment'></div>前后将吏军人百姓僧道等恳请为其帅置生祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376306_comment'></div>纪德政表章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376306_comment'></div>俾扬陟状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376306_comment'></div>宜允众情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376306_comment'></div>宰臣亦佥谓近镇大臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376306_comment'></div>谅能推心及物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376306_comment'></div>第因牢让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376306_comment'></div>久盖嘉庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376306_comment'></div>宜徵摭实之词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376306_comment'></div>用著不严之治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376306_comment'></div>翼日遂下诏前户部侍郎司空图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376306_comment'></div>条次所上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376306_comment'></div>刊示无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376306_comment'></div>谨按华州节度使太尉颍川郡王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1376306_comment'></div>许昌人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1376306_comment'></div>汝颖标奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1376306_comment'></div>勋华袭焕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1376306_comment'></div>伟登坛而挺佐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1376306_comment'></div>壮柱国以连荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1376306_comment'></div>间气迥钟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1376306_comment'></div>英材卓振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1376306_comment'></div>镇为岑鼎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1376306_comment'></div>用作雄铓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1376306_comment'></div>志不急于封侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1376306_comment'></div>誓惟坚于效节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1376306_comment'></div>累陈秘策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1376306_comment'></div>俄领偏师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1376306_comment'></div>洁身而遽出险中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1376306_comment'></div>振迹而旋归行在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1376306_comment'></div>详观机变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1376306_comment'></div>乃控河潼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1376306_comment'></div>既申匡复之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1376306_comment'></div>实显肃清之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1376306_comment'></div>师徒自辑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1376306_comment'></div>都邑晏然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1376306_comment'></div>大驾旋回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1376306_comment'></div>宸衷乃眷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1376306_comment'></div>抚绥益至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1376306_comment'></div>疲瘵渐苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1376306_comment'></div>初王之至任所也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1376306_comment'></div>公署仅存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1376306_comment'></div>人烟殆绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1376306_comment'></div>昼静而狐狸傲视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1376306_comment'></div>风惊而鸡犬蔑闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1376306_comment'></div>王寝兴匪宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1376306_comment'></div>吏士相勉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1376306_comment'></div>山祇应祷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1376306_comment'></div>膏泽以时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1376306_comment'></div>稍实仓箱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1376306_comment'></div>渐知礼义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1376306_comment'></div>才逾期月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1376306_comment'></div>日复流移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1376306_comment'></div>儿童沿路而不惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1376306_comment'></div>草木罹霜而亦润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1376306_comment'></div>关畿无阻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1376306_comment'></div>旅次皆安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1376306_comment'></div>污莱尽辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1376306_comment'></div>甍宇兼培。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1376306_comment'></div>其新附土众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1376306_comment'></div>亦竞课农桑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1376306_comment'></div>凡资生聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1376306_comment'></div>莫不蕃息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1376306_comment'></div>加垦公私田若干顷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1376306_comment'></div>畜牧艺植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1376306_comment'></div>亦皆称足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1376306_comment'></div>但三县兵荒之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1376306_comment'></div>虽赖招怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1376306_comment'></div>数都节制之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1376306_comment'></div>必伸威略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1376306_comment'></div>匪招怀何以附众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1376306_comment'></div>匪威略何以安人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1376306_comment'></div>动则经戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1376306_comment'></div>静则济理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1376306_comment'></div>餐和自化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1376306_comment'></div>别为君子之营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1376306_comment'></div>伏顺无前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1376306_comment'></div>亦有诸侯之剑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1376306_comment'></div>其始王之入守京室也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1376306_comment'></div>商州程景思乘虚掩袭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1376306_comment'></div>欲恣<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_116_1376306", 1376306, "Clauses/116/Comments/0")'>攻凌</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1376306_comment'></div>公驰自青门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1376306_comment'></div>战于赤水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1376306_comment'></div>其蔡军临阵剪灭驱系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1376306_comment'></div>而王并解甲纵之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1376306_comment'></div>明年春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1376306_comment'></div>宗权复遣贼将围逼陕郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1376306_comment'></div>虢州刺史张存背陕迎降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1376306_comment'></div>旋又持疑搆隙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1376306_comment'></div>遂密表请状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1376306_comment'></div>部伍据关捍敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1376306_comment'></div>曾未浃旬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1376306_comment'></div>遽闻失守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1376306_comment'></div>蔡将张琢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1376306_comment'></div>席卷深入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1376306_comment'></div>兵近五千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1376306_comment'></div>王所统见军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1376306_comment'></div>不逾六百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1376306_comment'></div>率先士卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1376306_comment'></div>尽殪凶渠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1376306_comment'></div>不崇朝而复收州城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1376306_comment'></div>自此藩方<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_137_1376306", 1376306, "Clauses/137/Comments/0")'>改观</span>矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1376306_comment'></div>又交锋之暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1376306_comment'></div>恤物尤勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1376306_comment'></div>遗犊弃蚕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1376306_comment'></div>皆令<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_141_1376306", 1376306, "Clauses/141/Comments/0")'>护养</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1376306_comment'></div>扶羸挈幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1376306_comment'></div>免复惊奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1376306_comment'></div>斯乃稔其庶富。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1376306_comment'></div>及天师北征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1376306_comment'></div>招讨使以繄仰请行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1376306_comment'></div>指撝务重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1376306_comment'></div><span class='authorDate'>（898年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_11909_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_11909'><span id='poem_sentence_0_11909_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_11909'>今日家山同此恨，人归未得鹤归无。<div id='poem_sentence_1_11909_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_11909'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_11909_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=899&endYear=899')">899年</a>　孙合来拜访图。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=899&endYear=899')">899年</a>　陈用拙来拜访图，图有感于时世撰文。作品：《疑经》《疑经后述》<div id='poem_1376292' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376292' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376292?labeling=true' target='_blank'>疑经</a><span class='authorDate'>（899年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14662, "唐末", "司空图", "poem_title_1376292")'>司空图</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376292_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376292'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376292'>经曰天王使来求金。又曰求车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376292_comment'></div>岂天王之使。私有求于鲁耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376292_comment'></div>不然。传闻之误耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376292_comment'></div>若诸侯之使来求金。则谓求可矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376292_comment'></div>若致天子之命。徵于诸侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376292_comment'></div>其可谓之求耶。且率土之人与其货殖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376292_comment'></div>皆一人之所有。父之材守于其子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376292_comment'></div>则用否莫不恭命。其可谓之求乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376292_comment'></div>春秋之旨。尊君卑臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376292_comment'></div>岂圣人为鲁不为周耶。书云天王狩于河阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376292_comment'></div>尚为晋侯讳召天子。岂可不为周讳其过哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376292_comment'></div>纵天子制用失节。多取于诸侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376292_comment'></div>而欲垂诫。即书于周史可矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376292_comment'></div>若书于诸侯之史。是吝吝其货而侮王命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376292_comment'></div>王祭亦不供矣。必非圣人之文也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376292_comment'></div>必若王人责其稽命。曷不书曰天王使某责贡金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376292_comment'></div>傥以取金为不文。曷不曰天王使某来徵贡金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376292_comment'></div>亦讥在其中矣。以是愚疑仲尼书天王使来求金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376292_comment'></div>是使私自求而惩之也。不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376292_comment'></div>求与责文或相近。传写之误焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376292_comment'></div>不尔。何子夏之徒不能措一言哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376292_comment'></div>舍此而讥诃。皆小小者耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376292_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1376292_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1376293' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376293' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376293?labeling=true' target='_blank'>疑经后述</a><span class='authorDate'>（899年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14662, "唐末", "司空图", "poem_title_1376293")'>司空图</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376293_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376293'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376293'>愚为诗为文一也。所务得诸己而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376293_comment'></div>未尝摭拾前贤之谬误。然为儒證道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376293_comment'></div>又不可皆无也。尝得柳子厚封建论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376293_comment'></div>以为三王树置。盖势使之然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376293_comment'></div>又有是苌宏之辨。意其多于救时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376293_comment'></div>今夏县谷郤自淮南缄所著新文而至。愚雅以孙文不尚辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376293_comment'></div>待之颇易。及见其卜年论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376293_comment'></div>又<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1376293", 1376293, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>耸然</span>加敬。钟陵秀士陈用拙出其宗人岳所作春秋折衷论数十篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376293_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1376293", 1376293, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>赡博</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1376293", 1376293, "Clauses/16/Comments/1")'>精致</span>。足以下视两汉<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1376293", 1376293, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>迂儒</span>矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376293_comment'></div>因激刚肠。有诋经之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376293_comment'></div>亦疑经文误耳。盖亟于时病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376293_comment'></div>言或不得其中。亦欲鼓陈君之锐气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376293_comment'></div>当有以复于我耳。时光化中兴二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376293_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1376293_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=899&endYear=899')">899年</a>　图有文回陈用拙。作品：《复陈君后书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文也有可能作于下年。）</span><div id='poem_1376253' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376253' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376253?labeling=true' target='_blank'>复陈君后书</a><span class='authorDate'>（899年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14662, "唐末", "司空图", "poem_title_1376253")'>司空图</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376253_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376253'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376253'>吾既以疑经为后述矣。今年夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376253_comment'></div>陈君果复致累百言。且援谷梁之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376253_comment'></div>欲以质吾。吾熟视其书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376253_comment'></div>率意而答之。足下复所云云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376253_comment'></div>非不知也。且夫谓之求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376253_comment'></div>则固当偕受其讥矣。虽然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376253_comment'></div>舅姑之疾且馁。苟力不能制其悍妇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376253_comment'></div>则必羸其声。哀求于一饭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376253_comment'></div>岂忍诮之乎。吾本朝之臣耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376253_comment'></div>岂敢诲其苞茅不贡之渐耶。于载之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376253_comment'></div>必有知言者。不多谭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376253_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1376253_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=900&endYear=900')">900年8月</a>　图在其女婿家获览唐代著名书法理论家李嗣真的《续书品》和书法家徐浩的有关书法的评论，撰《书屏文》<div id='poem_1376259' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376259' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376259?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书屏记</a><span class='authorDate'>（900年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(14662, "唐末", "司空图", "poem_title_1376259")'>司空图</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376259_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376259'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376259'>人之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1376259", 1376259, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>格状</span>或峻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376259_comment'></div>其心必劲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376259_comment'></div>心之劲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376259_comment'></div>则视其笔迹亦足见其人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376259_comment'></div>历代入书品者八十一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376259_comment'></div>贤杰多在其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376259_comment'></div>不可诬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376259_comment'></div>国初欧虞之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376259_comment'></div>继有名公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376259_comment'></div>元和长庆间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376259_comment'></div>先大夫初以诗师友兵部卢公载从事于商于。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376259_comment'></div>因题纪唱和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376259_comment'></div>乃以书受知于裴公休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376259_comment'></div>辟倅钟陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376259_comment'></div>及徵拜侍御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376259_comment'></div>退居中条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376259_comment'></div>时李忻州戎亦以草隶著称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376259_comment'></div>为计吏在满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376259_comment'></div>因辍所宝徐公浩真迹一屏以为贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376259_comment'></div>凡四十二幅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376259_comment'></div>八体皆备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376259_comment'></div>所题多文选五言诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376259_comment'></div>其朔风动秋草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376259_comment'></div>边马有归心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376259_comment'></div>十数字或草或隶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376259_comment'></div>尤为精绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376259_comment'></div>或缀小简于其下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376259_comment'></div>记云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376259_comment'></div>怒猊抉石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376259_comment'></div>渴骥奔泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376259_comment'></div>可以视碧落矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376259_comment'></div>先公清旦披玩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376259_comment'></div>殆废寝食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376259_comment'></div>常属诫云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376259_comment'></div>正长诗英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376259_comment'></div>吏部笔力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376259_comment'></div>逸气相资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376259_comment'></div>奇功无迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376259_comment'></div>儒家之宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376259_comment'></div>莫踰此屏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376259_comment'></div>但二者皆美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376259_comment'></div>神物所窥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376259_comment'></div>必当夺璧于中流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376259_comment'></div>飞铓于烈火也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376259_comment'></div>殆非子孙之所可存耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376259_comment'></div>庚子岁遇乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376259_comment'></div>自虞邑居负之置于王城别业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376259_comment'></div>丙辰春正月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376259_comment'></div>陕军复入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376259_comment'></div>则前后所藏及佛道图记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376259_comment'></div>共七千四百卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1376259_comment'></div>与是屏皆为灰烬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1376259_comment'></div>痛哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1376259_comment'></div>今旅寓华下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1376259_comment'></div>于进士姚顗所居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1376259_comment'></div>获览书品及徐公评论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1376259_comment'></div>因感愤<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_56_1376259", 1376259, "Clauses/56/Comments/0")'>追述</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1376259_comment'></div>贻信后学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1376259_comment'></div>且冀精于赏览者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1376259_comment'></div>必将继有诠次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1376259_comment'></div>光化二年八月三日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1376259_comment'></div>泗水司空图衔涕撰录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1376259_comment'></div>谨记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_62_1376259_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=901&endYear=901')">901年</a>　不详。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='4e17cba3db4b46ea8165ab5e07617f7a_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=903&endYear=903')">903年</a>，67岁</div><div id='4e17cba3db4b46ea8165ab5e07617f7a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=903&endYear=903')">903年</a>　图约在春夏时，由淅上先回华阴，有诗。作品：《自郧乡北归》<div id='poem_11846' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_11846' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_11846'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_11846'>巴烟幂幂久萦恨，楚柳绵绵今送归。<div id='poem_sentence_0_11846_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_11846'>回避江边同去雁，莫教惊起错南飞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_11846_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_11846'></div><div
